var allProcessors = {
  string: stringProcessor,
  number: numberProcessor,
  boolean: booleanProcessor,
  bigint: bigintProcessor,
  symbol: symbolProcessor,
  null: nullProcessor,
  undefined: undefinedProcessor,
  void: voidProcessor,
  never: neverProcessor,
  any: anyProcessor,
  unknown: unknownProcessor,
  date: dateProcessor,
  enum: enumProcessor,
  literal: literalProcessor,
  nan: nanProcessor,
  template_literal: templateLiteralProcessor,
  file: fileProcessor,
  success: successProcessor,
  custom: customProcessor,
  function: functionProcessor,
  transform: transformProcessor,
  map: mapProcessor,
  set: setProcessor,
  array: arrayProcessor,
  object: objectProcessor,
  union: unionProcessor,
  intersection: intersectionProcessor,
  tuple: tupleProcessor,
  record: recordProcessor,
  nullable: nullableProcessor,
  nonoptional: nonoptionalProcessor,
  default: defaultProcessor,
  prefault: prefaultProcessor,
  catch: catchProcessor,
  pipe: pipeProcessor,
  readonly: readonlyProcessor,
  promise: promiseProcessor,
  optional: optionalProcessor,
  lazy: lazyProcessor
};
function toJSONSchema(input, params) {
  if ("_idmap" in input) {
    const registry2 = input;
    const ctx2 = initializeContext({ ...params, processors: allProcessors });
    const defs = {};
    for (const entry of registry2._idmap.entries()) {
      const [_, schema] = entry;
      process(schema, ctx2);
    }
    const schemas = {};
    const external = {
      registry: registry2,
      uri: params?.uri,
      defs
    };
    ctx2.external = external;
    for (const entry of registry2._idmap.entries()) {
      const [key, schema] = entry;
      extractDefs(ctx2, schema);
      schemas[key] = finalize(ctx2, schema);
    }
    if (Object.keys(defs).length > 0) {
      const defsSegment = ctx2.target === "draft-2020-12" ? "$defs" : "definitions";
      schemas.__shared = {
        [defsSegment]: defs
      };
    }
    return { schemas };
  }
  const ctx = initializeContext({ ...params, processors: allProcessors });
  process(input, ctx);
  extractDefs(ctx, input);
  return finalize(ctx, input);
}
__name(toJSONSchema, "toJSONSchema");

// node_modules/zod/v4/core/json-schema-generator.js
var JSONSchemaGenerator = class {
  static {
    __name(this, "JSONSchemaGenerator");
  }
  /** @deprecated Access via ctx instead */
  get metadataRegistry() {
    return this.ctx.metadataRegistry;
  }
  /** @deprecated Access via ctx instead */
  get target() {
    return this.ctx.target;
  }
  /** @deprecated Access via ctx instead */
  get unrepresentable() {
    return this.ctx.unrepresentable;
  }
  /** @deprecated Access via ctx instead */
  get override() {
    return this.ctx.override;
  }
  /** @deprecated Access via ctx instead */
  get io() {
    return this.ctx.io;
  }
  /** @deprecated Access via ctx instead */
  get counter() {
    return this.ctx.counter;
  }
  set counter(value) {
    this.ctx.counter = value;
  }
  /** @deprecated Access via ctx instead */
  get seen() {
    return this.ctx.seen;
  }
  constructor(params) {
    let normalizedTarget = params?.target ?? "draft-2020-12";
    if (normalizedTarget === "draft-4")
      normalizedTarget = "draft-04";
    if (normalizedTarget === "draft-7")
      normalizedTarget = "draft-07";
    this.ctx = initializeContext({
      processors: allProcessors,
      target: normalizedTarget,
      ...params?.metadata && { metadata: params.metadata },
      ...params?.unrepresentable && { unrepresentable: params.unrepresentable },
      ...params?.override && { override: params.override },
      ...params?.io && { io: params.io }
    });
  }
  /**
   * Process a schema to prepare it for JSON Schema generation.
   * This must be called before emit().
   */
  process(schema, _params = { path: [], schemaPath: [] }) {
    return process(schema, this.ctx, _params);
  }
  /**
   * Emit the final JSON Schema after processing.
   * Must call process() first.
   */
  emit(schema, _params) {
    if (_params) {
      if (_params.cycles)
        this.ctx.cycles = _params.cycles;
      if (_params.reused)
        this.ctx.reused = _params.reused;
      if (_params.external)
        this.ctx.external = _params.external;
    }
    extractDefs(this.ctx, schema);
    const result = finalize(this.ctx, schema);
    const { "~standard": _, ...plainResult } = result;
    return plainResult;
  }
};

      configurable: true,
      enumerable: false,

        Object.defineProperty(this, key, {
          configurable: true,
          writable: true,
          enumerable: true,
          value: bound

      },

          configurable: true,
          writable: true,
          enumerable: true,

  }

var ZodEnum = /* @__PURE__ */ $constructor("ZodEnum", (inst, def) => {
  $ZodEnum.init(inst, def);
  ZodType.init(inst, def);
  inst._zod.processJSONSchema = (ctx, json2, params) => enumProcessor(inst, ctx, json2, params);
  inst.enum = def.entries;
  inst.options = Object.values(def.entries);
  const keys = new Set(Object.keys(def.entries));
  inst.extract = (values, params) => {
    const newEntries = {};
    for (const value of values) {
      if (keys.has(value)) {
        newEntries[value] = def.entries[value];
      } else
        throw new Error(`Key ${value} not found in enum`);
    }
    return new ZodEnum({
      ...def,
      checks: [],
      ...util_exports.normalizeParams(params),
      entries: newEntries
    });
  };
  inst.exclude = (values, params) => {
    const newEntries = { ...def.entries };
    for (const value of values) {
      if (keys.has(value)) {
        delete newEntries[value];
      } else
        throw new Error(`Key ${value} not found in enum`);
    }
    return new ZodEnum({
      ...def,
      checks: [],
      ...util_exports.normalizeParams(params),
      entries: newEntries
    });
  };
});

var ZodTransform = /* @__PURE__ */ $constructor("ZodTransform", (inst, def) => {
  $ZodTransform.init(inst, def);
  ZodType.init(inst, def);
  inst._zod.processJSONSchema = (ctx, json2, params) => transformProcessor(inst, ctx, json2, params);
  inst._zod.parse = (payload, _ctx) => {
    if (_ctx.direction === "backward") {
      throw new $ZodEncodeError(inst.constructor.name);
    }
    payload.addIssue = (issue2) => {
      if (typeof issue2 === "string") {
        payload.issues.push(util_exports.issue(issue2, payload.value, def));
      } else {
        const _issue = issue2;
        if (_issue.fatal)
          _issue.continue = false;
        _issue.code ?? (_issue.code = "custom");
        _issue.input ?? (_issue.input = payload.value);
        _issue.inst ?? (_issue.inst = inst);
        payload.issues.push(util_exports.issue(_issue));
      }
    };
    const output = def.transform(payload.value, payload);
    if (output instanceof Promise) {
      return output.then((output2) => {
        payload.value = output2;
        payload.fallback = true;
        return payload;
      });
    }
    payload.value = output;
    payload.fallback = true;
    return payload;

var z = {

var RECOGNIZED_KEYS = /* @__PURE__ */ new Set([
  // Schema identification
  "$schema",

  "definitions",

function detectVersion(schema, defaultTarget) {
  const $schema = schema.$schema;
  if ($schema === "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema") {
    return "draft-2020-12";
  }
  if ($schema === "http://json-schema.org/draft-07/schema#") {
    return "draft-7";
  }
  if ($schema === "http://json-schema.org/draft-04/schema#") {
    return "draft-4";
  }
  return defaultTarget ?? "draft-2020-12";
}
__name(detectVersion, "detectVersion");
function resolveRef(ref, ctx) {
  if (!ref.startsWith("#")) {
    throw new Error("External $ref is not supported, only local refs (#/...) are allowed");
  }
  const path = ref.slice(1).split("/").filter(Boolean);
  if (path.length === 0) {
    return ctx.rootSchema;
  }
  const defsKey = ctx.version === "draft-2020-12" ? "$defs" : "definitions";
  if (path[0] === defsKey) {
    const key = path[1];
    if (!key || !ctx.defs[key]) {
      throw new Error(`Reference not found: ${ref}`);
    }
    return ctx.defs[key];
  }
  throw new Error(`Reference not found: ${ref}`);
}
__name(resolveRef, "resolveRef");
function convertBaseSchema(schema, ctx) {
  if (schema.not !== void 0) {
    if (typeof schema.not === "object" && Object.keys(schema.not).length === 0) {
      return z.never();
    }
    throw new Error("not is not supported in Zod (except { not: {} } for never)");
  }
  if (schema.unevaluatedItems !== void 0) {
    throw new Error("unevaluatedItems is not supported");
  }
  if (schema.unevaluatedProperties !== void 0) {
    throw new Error("unevaluatedProperties is not supported");
  }
  if (schema.if !== void 0 || schema.then !== void 0 || schema.else !== void 0) {
    throw new Error("Conditional schemas (if/then/else) are not supported");
  }
  if (schema.dependentSchemas !== void 0 || schema.dependentRequired !== void 0) {
    throw new Error("dependentSchemas and dependentRequired are not supported");
  }
  if (schema.$ref) {
    const refPath = schema.$ref;
    if (ctx.refs.has(refPath)) {
      return ctx.refs.get(refPath);
    }
    if (ctx.processing.has(refPath)) {
      return z.lazy(() => {
        if (!ctx.refs.has(refPath)) {
          throw new Error(`Circular reference not resolved: ${refPath}`);
        }
        return ctx.refs.get(refPath);
      });
    }
    ctx.processing.add(refPath);
    const resolved = resolveRef(refPath, ctx);
    const zodSchema2 = convertSchema(resolved, ctx);
    ctx.refs.set(refPath, zodSchema2);
    ctx.processing.delete(refPath);
    return zodSchema2;
  }
  if (schema.enum !== void 0) {
    const enumValues = schema.enum;
    if (ctx.version === "openapi-3.0" && schema.nullable === true && enumValues.length === 1 && enumValues[0] === null) {
      return z.null();
    }
    if (enumValues.length === 0) {
      return z.never();
    }
    if (enumValues.length === 1) {
      return z.literal(enumValues[0]);
    }
    if (enumValues.every((v) => typeof v === "string")) {
      return z.enum(enumValues);
    }
    const literalSchemas = enumValues.map((v) => z.literal(v));
    if (literalSchemas.length < 2) {
      return literalSchemas[0];
    }
    return z.union([literalSchemas[0], literalSchemas[1], ...literalSchemas.slice(2)]);
  }
  if (schema.const !== void 0) {
    return z.literal(schema.const);
  }
  const type = schema.type;
  if (Array.isArray(type)) {
    const typeSchemas = type.map((t) => {
      const typeSchema = { ...schema, type: t };
      return convertBaseSchema(typeSchema, ctx);
    });
    if (typeSchemas.length === 0) {
      return z.never();
    }
    if (typeSchemas.length === 1) {
      return typeSchemas[0];
    }
    return z.union(typeSchemas);
  }
  if (!type) {
    return z.any();
  }
  let zodSchema;
  switch (type) {
    case "string": {
      let stringSchema = z.string();
      if (schema.format) {
        const format = schema.format;
        if (format === "email") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.email());
        } else if (format === "uri" || format === "uri-reference") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.url());
        } else if (format === "uuid" || format === "guid") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.uuid());
        } else if (format === "date-time") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.iso.datetime());
        } else if (format === "date") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.iso.date());
        } else if (format === "time") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.iso.time());
        } else if (format === "duration") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.iso.duration());
        } else if (format === "ipv4") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.ipv4());
        } else if (format === "ipv6") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.ipv6());
        } else if (format === "mac") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.mac());
        } else if (format === "cidr") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.cidrv4());
        } else if (format === "cidr-v6") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.cidrv6());
        } else if (format === "base64") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.base64());
        } else if (format === "base64url") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.base64url());
        } else if (format === "e164") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.e164());
        } else if (format === "jwt") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.jwt());
        } else if (format === "emoji") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.emoji());
        } else if (format === "nanoid") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.nanoid());
        } else if (format === "cuid") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.cuid());
        } else if (format === "cuid2") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.cuid2());
        } else if (format === "ulid") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.ulid());
        } else if (format === "xid") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.xid());
        } else if (format === "ksuid") {
          stringSchema = stringSchema.check(z.ksuid());
        }
      }
      if (typeof schema.minLength === "number") {
        stringSchema = stringSchema.min(schema.minLength);
      }
      if (typeof schema.maxLength === "number") {
        stringSchema = stringSchema.max(schema.maxLength);
      }
      if (schema.pattern) {
        stringSchema = stringSchema.regex(new RegExp(schema.pattern));
      }
      zodSchema = stringSchema;
      break;
    }
    case "number":
    case "integer": {
      let numberSchema = type === "integer" ? z.number().int() : z.number();
      if (typeof schema.minimum === "number") {
        numberSchema = numberSchema.min(schema.minimum);
      }
      if (typeof schema.maximum === "number") {
        numberSchema = numberSchema.max(schema.maximum);
      }
      if (typeof schema.exclusiveMinimum === "number") {
        numberSchema = numberSchema.gt(schema.exclusiveMinimum);
      } else if (schema.exclusiveMinimum === true && typeof schema.minimum === "number") {
        numberSchema = numberSchema.gt(schema.minimum);
      }
      if (typeof schema.exclusiveMaximum === "number") {
        numberSchema = numberSchema.lt(schema.exclusiveMaximum);
      } else if (schema.exclusiveMaximum === true && typeof schema.maximum === "number") {
        numberSchema = numberSchema.lt(schema.maximum);
      }
      if (typeof schema.multipleOf === "number") {
        numberSchema = numberSchema.multipleOf(schema.multipleOf);
      }
      zodSchema = numberSchema;
      break;
    }
    case "boolean": {
      zodSchema = z.boolean();
      break;
    }
    case "null": {
      zodSchema = z.null();
      break;
    }
    case "object": {
      const shape = {};
      const properties = schema.properties || {};
      const requiredSet = new Set(schema.required || []);
      for (const [key, propSchema] of Object.entries(properties)) {
        const propZodSchema = convertSchema(propSchema, ctx);
        shape[key] = requiredSet.has(key) ? propZodSchema : propZodSchema.optional();
      }
      if (schema.propertyNames) {
        const keySchema = convertSchema(schema.propertyNames, ctx);
        const valueSchema = schema.additionalProperties && typeof schema.additionalProperties === "object" ? convertSchema(schema.additionalProperties, ctx) : z.any();
        if (Object.keys(shape).length === 0) {
          zodSchema = z.record(keySchema, valueSchema);
          break;
        }
        const objectSchema2 = z.object(shape).passthrough();
        const recordSchema = z.looseRecord(keySchema, valueSchema);
        zodSchema = z.intersection(objectSchema2, recordSchema);
        break;
      }
      if (schema.patternProperties) {
        const patternProps = schema.patternProperties;
        const patternKeys = Object.keys(patternProps);
        const looseRecords = [];
        for (const pattern of patternKeys) {
          const patternValue = convertSchema(patternProps[pattern], ctx);
          const keySchema = z.string().regex(new RegExp(pattern));
          looseRecords.push(z.looseRecord(keySchema, patternValue));
        }
        const schemasToIntersect = [];
        if (Object.keys(shape).length > 0) {
          schemasToIntersect.push(z.object(shape).passthrough());
        }
        schemasToIntersect.push(...looseRecords);
        if (schemasToIntersect.length === 0) {
          zodSchema = z.object({}).passthrough();
        } else if (schemasToIntersect.length === 1) {
          zodSchema = schemasToIntersect[0];
        } else {
          let result = z.intersection(schemasToIntersect[0], schemasToIntersect[1]);
          for (let i = 2; i < schemasToIntersect.length; i++) {
            result = z.intersection(result, schemasToIntersect[i]);
          }
          zodSchema = result;
        }
        break;
      }
      const objectSchema = z.object(shape);
      if (schema.additionalProperties === false) {
        zodSchema = objectSchema.strict();
      } else if (typeof schema.additionalProperties === "object") {
        zodSchema = objectSchema.catchall(convertSchema(schema.additionalProperties, ctx));
      } else {
        zodSchema = objectSchema.passthrough();
      }
      break;
    }
    case "array": {
      const prefixItems = schema.prefixItems;
      const items = schema.items;
      if (prefixItems && Array.isArray(prefixItems)) {
        const tupleItems = prefixItems.map((item) => convertSchema(item, ctx));
        const rest = items && typeof items === "object" && !Array.isArray(items) ? convertSchema(items, ctx) : void 0;
        if (rest) {
          zodSchema = z.tuple(tupleItems).rest(rest);
        } else {
          zodSchema = z.tuple(tupleItems);
        }
        if (typeof schema.minItems === "number") {
          zodSchema = zodSchema.check(z.minLength(schema.minItems));
        }
        if (typeof schema.maxItems === "number") {
          zodSchema = zodSchema.check(z.maxLength(schema.maxItems));
        }
      } else if (Array.isArray(items)) {
        const tupleItems = items.map((item) => convertSchema(item, ctx));
        const rest = schema.additionalItems && typeof schema.additionalItems === "object" ? convertSchema(schema.additionalItems, ctx) : void 0;
        if (rest) {
          zodSchema = z.tuple(tupleItems).rest(rest);
        } else {
          zodSchema = z.tuple(tupleItems);
        }
        if (typeof schema.minItems === "number") {
          zodSchema = zodSchema.check(z.minLength(schema.minItems));
        }
        if (typeof schema.maxItems === "number") {
          zodSchema = zodSchema.check(z.maxLength(schema.maxItems));
        }
      } else if (items !== void 0) {
        const element = convertSchema(items, ctx);
        let arraySchema = z.array(element);
        if (typeof schema.minItems === "number") {
          arraySchema = arraySchema.min(schema.minItems);
        }
        if (typeof schema.maxItems === "number") {
          arraySchema = arraySchema.max(schema.maxItems);
        }
        zodSchema = arraySchema;
      } else {
        zodSchema = z.array(z.any());
      }
      break;
    }
    default:
      throw new Error(`Unsupported type: ${type}`);
  }
  return zodSchema;
}
__name(convertBaseSchema, "convertBaseSchema");
function convertSchema(schema, ctx) {
  if (typeof schema === "boolean") {
    return schema ? z.any() : z.never();
  }
  let baseSchema = convertBaseSchema(schema, ctx);
  const hasExplicitType = schema.type || schema.enum !== void 0 || schema.const !== void 0;
  if (schema.anyOf && Array.isArray(schema.anyOf)) {
    const options = schema.anyOf.map((s) => convertSchema(s, ctx));
    const anyOfUnion = z.union(options);
    baseSchema = hasExplicitType ? z.intersection(baseSchema, anyOfUnion) : anyOfUnion;
  }
  if (schema.oneOf && Array.isArray(schema.oneOf)) {
    const options = schema.oneOf.map((s) => convertSchema(s, ctx));
    const oneOfUnion = z.xor(options);
    baseSchema = hasExplicitType ? z.intersection(baseSchema, oneOfUnion) : oneOfUnion;
  }
  if (schema.allOf && Array.isArray(schema.allOf)) {
    if (schema.allOf.length === 0) {
      baseSchema = hasExplicitType ? baseSchema : z.any();
    } else {
      let result = hasExplicitType ? baseSchema : convertSchema(schema.allOf[0], ctx);
      const startIdx = hasExplicitType ? 0 : 1;
      for (let i = startIdx; i < schema.allOf.length; i++) {
        result = z.intersection(result, convertSchema(schema.allOf[i], ctx));
      }
      baseSchema = result;
    }
  }
  if (schema.nullable === true && ctx.version === "openapi-3.0") {
    baseSchema = z.nullable(baseSchema);
  }
  if (schema.readOnly === true) {
    baseSchema = z.readonly(baseSchema);
  }
  if (schema.default !== void 0) {
    baseSchema = baseSchema.default(schema.default);
  }
  const extraMeta = {};
  const coreMetadataKeys = ["$id", "id", "$comment", "$anchor", "$vocabulary", "$dynamicRef", "$dynamicAnchor"];
  for (const key of coreMetadataKeys) {
    if (key in schema) {
      extraMeta[key] = schema[key];
    }
  }
  const contentMetadataKeys = ["contentEncoding", "contentMediaType", "contentSchema"];
  for (const key of contentMetadataKeys) {
    if (key in schema) {
      extraMeta[key] = schema[key];
    }
  }
  for (const key of Object.keys(schema)) {
    if (!RECOGNIZED_KEYS.has(key)) {
      extraMeta[key] = schema[key];
    }
  }
  if (Object.keys(extraMeta).length > 0) {
    ctx.registry.add(baseSchema, extraMeta);
  }
  if (schema.description) {
    baseSchema = baseSchema.describe(schema.description);
  }
  return baseSchema;
}
__name(convertSchema, "convertSchema");
function fromJSONSchema(schema, params) {
  if (typeof schema === "boolean") {
    return schema ? z.any() : z.never();
  }
  let normalized;
  try {
    normalized = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(schema));
  } catch {
    throw new Error("fromJSONSchema input is not valid JSON (possibly cyclic); use $defs/$ref for recursive schemas");
  }
  const version3 = detectVersion(normalized, params?.defaultTarget);
  const defs = normalized.$defs || normalized.definitions || {};
  const ctx = {
    version: version3,
    defs,
    refs: /* @__PURE__ */ new Map(),
    processing: /* @__PURE__ */ new Set(),
    rootSchema: normalized,
    registry: params?.registry ?? globalRegistry
  };
  return convertSchema(normalized, ctx);
}
__name(fromJSONSchema, "fromJSONSchema");

// src/routes/requestBody.ts
var RequestBodyTooLargeError = class extends Error {
  static {
    __name(this, "RequestBodyTooLargeError");
  }
  maxBytes;
  constructor(maxBytes) {
    super(`Request body exceeds ${maxBytes} bytes`);
    this.name = "RequestBodyTooLargeError";
    this.maxBytes = maxBytes;
  }
};
function contentLengthExceedsLimit(request, maxBytes) {
  const contentLengthHeader = request.headers.get("content-length");
  if (contentLengthHeader === null) {
    return false;
  }
  const contentLength = Number(contentLengthHeader);
  return Number.isFinite(contentLength) && contentLength > maxBytes;
}
__name(contentLengthExceedsLimit, "contentLengthExceedsLimit");
async function readTextBodyWithLimit(request, maxBytes) {
  if (request.body === null) {
    return "";
  }
  const reader = request.body.getReader();
  const decoder = new TextDecoder();
  let byteCount = 0;
  let body = "";
  try {
    for (; ; ) {
      const chunk = await reader.read();
      if (chunk.done) {
        body += decoder.decode();
        return body;
      }
      byteCount += chunk.value.byteLength;
      if (byteCount > maxBytes) {
        await reader.cancel();
        throw new RequestBodyTooLargeError(maxBytes);
      }
      body += decoder.decode(chunk.value, { stream: true });
    }
  } finally {
    reader.releaseLock();
  }
}
__name(readTextBodyWithLimit, "readTextBodyWithLimit");

// src/routes/admin/shared.ts
async function requireAdminToken(c) {
  const authResult = await verifyAdminToken({
    expectedTokenHash: c.env.TM_ADMIN_TOKEN_HASH,
    suppliedToken: c.req.header(ADMIN_TOKEN_HEADER)
  });
  if (authResult.ok) {
    return null;
  }
  return buildAdminRejectedResponse("unauthorized", 401);
}
__name(requireAdminToken, "requireAdminToken");
async function readAdminJsonBody(c) {
  const contentType = c.req.header("Content-Type") ?? "";
  if (!contentType.toLowerCase().includes("application/json")) {
    return {
      ok: false,
      response: buildAdminRejectedResponse("unsupported_media_type", 415)
    };
  }
  if (contentLengthExceedsLimit(
    c.req.raw,
    ADMIN_DEVICE_REQUEST_LIMITS.maxRawBodyBytes
  )) {
    return {
      ok: false,
      response: buildAdminRejectedResponse("payload_too_large", 413)
    };
  }
  let rawBody;
  try {
    rawBody = await readTextBodyWithLimit(
      c.req.raw,
      ADMIN_DEVICE_REQUEST_LIMITS.maxRawBodyBytes
    );
  } catch (error51) {
    if (error51 instanceof RequestBodyTooLargeError) {
      return {
        ok: false,
        response: buildAdminRejectedResponse("payload_too_large", 413)
      };
    }
    throw error51;
  }
  try {
    return { ok: true, body: JSON.parse(rawBody) };
  } catch {
    return {
      ok: false,
      response: buildAdminRejectedResponse("invalid_request", 400)
    };
  }
}
__name(readAdminJsonBody, "readAdminJsonBody");
function buildAdminRejectedResponse(reason, status) {
  const responseBody = {
    status: "rejected",
    reason
  };
  return nonCacheableJson(
    responseBody,
    { status }
  );
}
__name(buildAdminRejectedResponse, "buildAdminRejectedResponse");

  const responseBody = {
    status: "not_found",

  };
  return nonCacheableJson(
    responseBody,
    { status: 404 }
  );
}

// src/routes/admin/batches.ts
async function handleAdminDeviceBatches(c) {
  const authFailure = await requireAdminToken(c);
  if (authFailure !== null) {
    return authFailure;
  }
  const deviceId = parseAdminPathDeviceId(c);
  if (deviceId === null) {
    return buildAdminRejectedResponse("invalid_request", 400);
  }
  const device = await loadDeviceInspectionByDeviceId(c.env.DB, deviceId);
  if (device === null) {
    return buildAdminNotFoundResponse(deviceId);
  }
  const batches = await loadRecentIngestBatchesByDeviceId(c.env.DB, deviceId);
  const responseBody = {
    status: "ok",
    device_id: deviceId,
    count: batches.length,
    limit: ADMIN_INGEST_BATCH_LIST_LIMIT,
    batches: batches.map(formatInspectableIngestBatch)
  };
  return nonCacheableJson(responseBody);
}
__name(handleAdminDeviceBatches, "handleAdminDeviceBatches");
async function handleAdminDeviceBatchInspection(c) {
  const authFailure = await requireAdminToken(c);
  if (authFailure !== null) {
    return authFailure;
  }
  const deviceId = parseAdminPathDeviceId(c);
  const batchId = parseAdminPathBatchId(c);
  if (deviceId === null || batchId === null) {
    return buildAdminRejectedResponse("invalid_request", 400);
  }
  const batch = await loadIngestBatchInspectionByDeviceAndBatchId(
    c.env.DB,
    deviceId,
    batchId
  );
  if (batch === null) {
    return buildAdminBatchNotFoundResponse(deviceId, batchId);
  }
  const measurementSummary = await loadMeasurementSummaryForBatchRange(
    c.env.DB,
    {
      deviceId: batch.deviceId,
      profile: batch.profile,
      seqFirst: batch.seqFirst,
      seqLast: batch.seqLast
    }
  );
  const batchDetail = {
    ...formatInspectableIngestBatch(batch),
    measurement_summary: formatMeasurementSummary(measurementSummary)
  };
  const responseBody = {
    status: "ok",
    batch: batchDetail
  };
  return nonCacheableJson(responseBody);
}
__name(handleAdminDeviceBatchInspection, "handleAdminDeviceBatchInspection");
async function handleAdminDeviceBatchRawPayload(c) {
  const authFailure = await requireAdminToken(c);
  if (authFailure !== null) {
    return authFailure;
  }
  const deviceId = parseAdminPathDeviceId(c);
  const batchId = parseAdminPathBatchId(c);
  if (deviceId === null || batchId === null) {
    return buildAdminRejectedResponse("invalid_request", 400);
  }
  const batch = await loadIngestBatchInspectionByDeviceAndBatchId(
    c.env.DB,
    deviceId,
    batchId
  );
  if (batch === null) {
    return buildAdminBatchNotFoundResponse(deviceId, batchId);
  }
  const rawPayload = await loadRawBatchPayload(
    c.env.RAW_BATCHES,
    batch.rawR2Key
  );
  if (rawPayload === null) {
    return buildAdminRejectedResponse("raw_payload_missing", 404);
  }
  const rawPayloadSha256 = await sha256Hex(rawPayload);
  if (rawPayloadSha256 !== batch.rawPayloadSha256) {
    return buildAdminRejectedResponse("raw_payload_hash_mismatch", 409);
  }
  const headers = new Headers({
    "Content-Type": "application/json; charset=utf-8",
    "Content-Disposition": `attachment; filename="${buildRawBatchJsonFilename(deviceId, batchId)}"`,
    "X-Content-Type-Options": "nosniff",
    "X-TM-Raw-Payload-Sha256": batch.rawPayloadSha256
  });
  return nonCacheableResponse(rawPayload, { headers });
}
__name(handleAdminDeviceBatchRawPayload, "handleAdminDeviceBatchRawPayload");
function buildRawBatchJsonFilename(deviceId, batchId) {
  return `tunnel-monitor-${safeFilenameSegment(deviceId)}-${safeFilenameSegment(batchId)}.json`;
}
__name(buildRawBatchJsonFilename, "buildRawBatchJsonFilename");
function safeFilenameSegment(value) {
  const segment = value.replaceAll(/[^A-Za-z0-9._-]+/g, "_");
  return segment.length > 0 ? segment : "unknown";
}
__name(safeFilenameSegment, "safeFilenameSegment");

async function handleAdminDeviceCreate(c) {
  const authFailure = await requireAdminToken(c);
  if (authFailure !== null) {
    return authFailure;
  }
  const requestBody = await readAdminJsonBody(c);
  if (!requestBody.ok) {
    return requestBody.response;
  }
  const parsedRequest = safeParseCreateAdminDeviceRequest(requestBody.body);
  if (!parsedRequest.success) {
    return buildAdminRejectedResponse("invalid_request", 400);
  }
  const tokenHash = await sha256Hex(parsedRequest.data.token);
  const createResult = await createDeviceRegistration(c.env.DB, {
    deviceId: parsedRequest.data.device_id,
    tokenHash,
    displayName: parsedRequest.data.display_name,
    active: parsedRequest.data.active,
    configRevision: parsedRequest.data.config_revision,
    createdAt: /* @__PURE__ */ new Date()
  });
  if (!createResult.created) {
    return buildAdminRejectedResponse(createResult.reason, 409);
  }
  const device = await loadDeviceInspectionByDeviceId(
    c.env.DB,
    parsedRequest.data.device_id
  );
  if (device === null) {
    throw new Error("Created device registration could not be loaded");
  }
  const responseBody = {
    status: "created",
    device: formatInspectableDevice(device)
  };
  return nonCacheableJson(
    responseBody,
    { status: 201 }
  );
}
__name(handleAdminDeviceCreate, "handleAdminDeviceCreate");

async function handleAdminDeviceUpdate(c) {
  const authFailure = await requireAdminToken(c);
  if (authFailure !== null) {
    return authFailure;
  }
  const deviceId = parseAdminPathDeviceId(c);
  if (deviceId === null) {
    return buildAdminRejectedResponse("invalid_request", 400);
  }
  const requestBody = await readAdminJsonBody(c);
  if (!requestBody.ok) {
    return requestBody.response;
  }
  const parsedRequest = safeParseUpdateAdminDeviceRequest(requestBody.body);
  if (!parsedRequest.success) {
    return buildAdminRejectedResponse("invalid_request", 400);
  }
  const updated = await updateDeviceRegistration(c.env.DB, {
    deviceId,
    tokenHash: parsedRequest.data.token === void 0 ? void 0 : await sha256Hex(parsedRequest.data.token),
    displayName: parsedRequest.data.display_name,
    active: parsedRequest.data.active,
    configRevision: parsedRequest.data.config_revision
  });
  if (!updated) {
    return buildAdminNotFoundResponse(deviceId);
  }
  const device = await loadDeviceInspectionByDeviceId(c.env.DB, deviceId);
  if (device === null) {
    return buildAdminNotFoundResponse(deviceId);
  }
  const responseBody = {
    status: "ok",
    device: formatInspectableDevice(device)
  };
  return nonCacheableJson(responseBody);
}
__name(handleAdminDeviceUpdate, "handleAdminDeviceUpdate");

__name(decodeAdminMeasurementSeriesCursor, "decodeAdminMeasurementSeriesCursor");
function encodeCursorPayload(payload) {
  const bytes = new TextEncoder().encode(JSON.stringify(payload));
  let binary = "";
  for (const byte of bytes) {
    binary += String.fromCharCode(byte);
  }
  return btoa(binary).replaceAll("+", "-").replaceAll("/", "_").replaceAll("=", "");
}
__name(encodeCursorPayload, "encodeCursorPayload");
function decodeCursorPayload(value) {
  try {
    const base643 = value.replaceAll("-", "+").replaceAll("_", "/");
    const paddedBase64 = base643.padEnd(Math.ceil(base643.length / 4) * 4, "=");
    const binary = atob(paddedBase64);
    const bytes = Uint8Array.from(
      binary,
      (character) => character.charCodeAt(0)
    );
    return JSON.parse(new TextDecoder().decode(bytes));
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}
__name(decodeCursorPayload, "decodeCursorPayload");

// src/admin/measurementRequests.ts
var integerQueryParamSchema = external_exports.string().regex(/^-?\d+$/).transform((value) => Number(value)).pipe(external_exports.number().int());

  external_exports.number().int().min(1).max(ADMIN_MEASUREMENT_QUERY_LIMITS.maxLimit)

  external_exports.number().int().min(1).max(ADMIN_MEASUREMENT_SERIES_QUERY_LIMITS.maxLimit)
);
var metricFilterSchema = external_exports.string().min(1).max(ADMIN_MEASUREMENT_QUERY_LIMITS.maxMetricLength);
var measurementSeriesXAxisSchema = external_exports.enum(MEASUREMENT_SERIES_X_AXES);
var measurementCursorQueryParamSchema = external_exports.string().min(1).max(ADMIN_MEASUREMENT_CURSOR_LIMITS.maxEncodedLength).transform((value, context) => {
  const cursor = decodeAdminMeasurementCursor(value);
  if (cursor === null) {
    context.addIssue({
      code: "custom",
      message: "invalid measurement cursor"
    });
    return external_exports.NEVER;
  }
  return cursor;
});
var measurementSeriesCursorQueryParamSchema = external_exports.string().min(1).max(ADMIN_MEASUREMENT_CURSOR_LIMITS.maxEncodedLength).transform((value, context) => {
  const cursor = decodeAdminMeasurementSeriesCursor(value);
  if (cursor === null) {
    context.addIssue({
      code: "custom",
      message: "invalid measurement series cursor"
    });
    return external_exports.NEVER;
  }
  return cursor;
});
var adminMeasurementQuerySchema = external_exports.object({
  metric: metricFilterSchema.optional(),
  metric_prefix: metricFilterSchema.optional(),
  seq_from: integerQueryParamSchema.optional(),
  seq_to: integerQueryParamSchema.optional(),
  limit: measurementListLimitQueryParamSchema.optional(),
  cursor: measurementCursorQueryParamSchema.optional()
}).strict().superRefine((query, context) => {
  if (query.metric !== void 0 && query.metric_prefix !== void 0) {
    context.addIssue({
      code: "custom",
      message: "metric and metric_prefix cannot be used together",
      path: ["metric"]
    });
  }
  if (query.seq_from !== void 0 && query.seq_to !== void 0 && query.seq_from > query.seq_to) {
    context.addIssue({
      code: "custom",
      message: "seq_from cannot be greater than seq_to",
      path: ["seq_from"]
    });
  }
}).transform((query) => {
  return {
    metric: query.metric ?? null,
    metricPrefix: query.metric_prefix ?? null,
    seqFrom: query.seq_from ?? null,
    seqTo: query.seq_to ?? null,
    limit: query.limit ?? ADMIN_MEASUREMENT_QUERY_LIMITS.defaultLimit,
    cursor: query.cursor ?? null
  };
});
var adminMeasurementSeriesQuerySchema = external_exports.object({
  metric: metricFilterSchema,
  x_axis: measurementSeriesXAxisSchema.optional(),
  seq_from: integerQueryParamSchema.optional(),
  seq_to: integerQueryParamSchema.optional(),
  sample_time_from: integerQueryParamSchema.optional(),
  sample_time_to: integerQueryParamSchema.optional(),
  limit: measurementSeriesLimitQueryParamSchema.optional(),
  cursor: measurementSeriesCursorQueryParamSchema.optional()
}).strict().superRefine((query, context) => {
  if (query.seq_from !== void 0 && query.seq_to !== void 0 && query.seq_from > query.seq_to) {
    context.addIssue({
      code: "custom",
      message: "seq_from cannot be greater than seq_to",
      path: ["seq_from"]
    });
  }
  if (query.sample_time_from !== void 0 && query.sample_time_to !== void 0 && query.sample_time_from > query.sample_time_to) {
    context.addIssue({
      code: "custom",
      message: "sample_time_from cannot be greater than sample_time_to",
      path: ["sample_time_from"]
    });
  }
  if (query.cursor !== void 0 && query.cursor.xAxis !== (query.x_axis ?? "seq")) {
    context.addIssue({
      code: "custom",
      message: "cursor x_axis does not match query x_axis",
      path: ["cursor"]
    });
  }
}).transform((query) => {
  return {
    metric: query.metric,
    xAxis: query.x_axis ?? "seq",
    seqFrom: query.seq_from ?? null,
    seqTo: query.seq_to ?? null,
    sampleTimeFrom: query.sample_time_from ?? null,
    sampleTimeTo: query.sample_time_to ?? null,
    limit: query.limit ?? ADMIN_MEASUREMENT_SERIES_QUERY_LIMITS.defaultLimit,
    cursor: query.cursor ?? null
  };
});
function safeParseAdminMeasurementQuery(searchParams) {
  if (hasDuplicateQueryKeys(searchParams)) {
    return adminMeasurementQuerySchema.safeParse({
      unsupported_duplicate_query_key: true
    });
  }
  return adminMeasurementQuerySchema.safeParse(
    queryParamsToPlainObject(searchParams)
  );
}
__name(safeParseAdminMeasurementQuery, "safeParseAdminMeasurementQuery");
function safeParseAdminMeasurementSeriesQuery(searchParams) {
  if (hasDuplicateQueryKeys(searchParams)) {
    return adminMeasurementSeriesQuerySchema.safeParse({
      unsupported_duplicate_query_key: true
    });
  }
  return adminMeasurementSeriesQuerySchema.safeParse(
    queryParamsToPlainObject(searchParams)
  );
}
__name(safeParseAdminMeasurementSeriesQuery, "safeParseAdminMeasurementSeriesQuery");
function hasDuplicateQueryKeys(searchParams) {
  const seenKeys = /* @__PURE__ */ new Set();
  for (const key of searchParams.keys()) {
    if (seenKeys.has(key)) {
      return true;
    }
    seenKeys.add(key);
  }
  return false;
}
__name(hasDuplicateQueryKeys, "hasDuplicateQueryKeys");
function queryParamsToPlainObject(searchParams) {
  const query = {};
  for (const [key, value] of searchParams) {
    query[key] = value;
  }
  return query;
}
__name(queryParamsToPlainObject, "queryParamsToPlainObject");

// src/routes/admin/csv.ts
var MEASUREMENT_SERIES_CSV_COLUMNS = [
  "device_id",
  "metric",
  "unit",
  "seq",
  "sample_time",
  "value"
];
function formatMeasurementSeriesCsv(input) {
  const rows = [
    MEASUREMENT_SERIES_CSV_COLUMNS,
    ...input.points.map((point) => [
      input.deviceId,
      input.metric,
      point.unit,
      point.seq,
      point.sampleTime,
      point.value
    ])
  ];
  return `${rows.map(formatCsvRow).join("\r\n")}\r
`;
}
__name(formatMeasurementSeriesCsv, "formatMeasurementSeriesCsv");
function buildMeasurementSeriesCsvFilename(deviceId, metric) {
  return `tunnel-monitor-${safeFilenameSegment2(deviceId)}-${safeFilenameSegment2(metric)}.csv`;
}
__name(buildMeasurementSeriesCsvFilename, "buildMeasurementSeriesCsvFilename");
function formatCsvRow(values) {
  return values.map(formatCsvCell).join(",");
}
__name(formatCsvRow, "formatCsvRow");
function formatCsvCell(value) {
  if (value === null) {
    return "";
  }
  const text2 = String(value);
  if (!/[",\r\n]/.test(text2)) {
    return text2;
  }
  return `"${text2.replaceAll('"', '""')}"`;
}
__name(formatCsvCell, "formatCsvCell");
function safeFilenameSegment2(value) {
  const segment = value.replaceAll(/[^A-Za-z0-9._-]+/g, "_");
  return segment.length > 0 ? segment : "unknown";
}
__name(safeFilenameSegment2, "safeFilenameSegment");

// src/routes/admin/measurements.ts
async function handleAdminDeviceMeasurements(c) {
  const authFailure = await requireAdminToken(c);
  if (authFailure !== null) {
    return authFailure;
  }
  const deviceId = parseAdminPathDeviceId(c);
  if (deviceId === null) {
    return buildAdminRejectedResponse("invalid_request", 400);
  }
  const parsedQuery = safeParseAdminMeasurementQuery(
    new URL(c.req.url).searchParams
  );
  if (!parsedQuery.success) {
    return buildAdminRejectedResponse("invalid_request", 400);
  }
  const device = await loadDeviceInspectionByDeviceId(c.env.DB, deviceId);
  if (device === null) {
    return buildAdminNotFoundResponse(deviceId);
  }
  const requestedLimit = parsedQuery.data.limit;
  const measurements2 = await listMeasurementsForDevice(c.env.DB, {
    deviceId,
    metric: parsedQuery.data.metric,
    metricPrefix: parsedQuery.data.metricPrefix,
    seqFrom: parsedQuery.data.seqFrom,
    seqTo: parsedQuery.data.seqTo,
    limit: requestedLimit + 1,
    cursor: parsedQuery.data.cursor
  });
  const returnedMeasurements = measurements2.slice(0, requestedLimit);
  const hasMore = measurements2.length > requestedLimit;
  const responseBody = {
    status: "ok",
    device_id: deviceId,
    returned_count: returnedMeasurements.length,
    limit: requestedLimit,
    has_more: hasMore,
    next_cursor: buildNextMeasurementCursor(returnedMeasurements, hasMore),
    filters: formatAdminMeasurementQueryFilters(parsedQuery.data),
    measurements: returnedMeasurements.map(formatInspectableMeasurement)
  };
  return nonCacheableJson(responseBody);
}
__name(handleAdminDeviceMeasurements, "handleAdminDeviceMeasurements");
async function handleAdminDeviceMeasurementMetrics(c) {
  const authFailure = await requireAdminToken(c);
  if (authFailure !== null) {
    return authFailure;
  }
  const deviceId = parseAdminPathDeviceId(c);
  if (deviceId === null) {
    return buildAdminRejectedResponse("invalid_request", 400);
  }
  const device = await loadDeviceInspectionByDeviceId(c.env.DB, deviceId);
  if (device === null) {
    return buildAdminNotFoundResponse(deviceId);
  }
  const metrics = await listMeasurementMetricsForDevice(c.env.DB, deviceId);
  const responseBody = {
    status: "ok",
    device_id: deviceId,
    count: metrics.length,
    metrics: metrics.map(formatMeasurementMetricSummary)
  };
  return nonCacheableJson(responseBody);
}
__name(handleAdminDeviceMeasurementMetrics, "handleAdminDeviceMeasurementMetrics");
async function handleAdminDeviceMeasurementSeries(c) {
  const authFailure = await requireAdminToken(c);
  if (authFailure !== null) {
    return authFailure;
  }
  const deviceId = parseAdminPathDeviceId(c);
  if (deviceId === null) {
    return buildAdminRejectedResponse("invalid_request", 400);
  }
  const parsedQuery = safeParseAdminMeasurementSeriesQuery(
    new URL(c.req.url).searchParams
  );
  if (!parsedQuery.success) {
    return buildAdminRejectedResponse("invalid_request", 400);
  }
  const device = await loadDeviceInspectionByDeviceId(c.env.DB, deviceId);
  if (device === null) {
    return buildAdminNotFoundResponse(deviceId);
  }
  const requestedLimit = parsedQuery.data.limit;
  const seriesPage = await loadAdminMeasurementSeriesPage(
    c.env.DB,
    deviceId,
    parsedQuery.data
  );
  const responseBody = {
    status: "ok",
    device_id: deviceId,
    metric: parsedQuery.data.metric,
    unit: seriesPage.returnedPoints[0]?.unit ?? null,
    x_axis: parsedQuery.data.xAxis,
    returned_count: seriesPage.returnedPoints.length,
    limit: requestedLimit,
    has_more: seriesPage.hasMore,
    next_cursor: seriesPage.nextCursor,
    filters: formatAdminMeasurementSeriesQueryFilters(parsedQuery.data),
    points: seriesPage.returnedPoints.map(formatMeasurementSeriesPoint)
  };
  return nonCacheableJson(responseBody);
}
__name(handleAdminDeviceMeasurementSeries, "handleAdminDeviceMeasurementSeries");
async function handleAdminDeviceMeasurementSeriesCsv(c) {
  const authFailure = await requireAdminToken(c);
  if (authFailure !== null) {
    return authFailure;
  }
  const deviceId = parseAdminPathDeviceId(c);
  if (deviceId === null) {
    return buildAdminRejectedResponse("invalid_request", 400);
  }
  const parsedQuery = safeParseAdminMeasurementSeriesQuery(
    new URL(c.req.url).searchParams
  );
  if (!parsedQuery.success) {
    return buildAdminRejectedResponse("invalid_request", 400);
  }
  const device = await loadDeviceInspectionByDeviceId(c.env.DB, deviceId);
  if (device === null) {
    return buildAdminNotFoundResponse(deviceId);
  }
  const seriesPage = await loadAdminMeasurementSeriesPage(
    c.env.DB,
    deviceId,
    parsedQuery.data
  );
  const csv = formatMeasurementSeriesCsv({
    deviceId,
    metric: parsedQuery.data.metric,
    points: seriesPage.returnedPoints
  });
  const headers = new Headers({
    "Content-Type": "text/csv; charset=utf-8",
    "Content-Disposition": `attachment; filename="${buildMeasurementSeriesCsvFilename(deviceId, parsedQuery.data.metric)}"`,
    "X-TM-Returned-Count": String(seriesPage.returnedPoints.length),
    "X-TM-Limit": String(parsedQuery.data.limit),
    "X-TM-Has-More": String(seriesPage.hasMore)
  });
  if (seriesPage.nextCursor !== null) {
    headers.set("X-TM-Next-Cursor", seriesPage.nextCursor);
  }
  return nonCacheableResponse(csv, { headers });
}
__name(handleAdminDeviceMeasurementSeriesCsv, "handleAdminDeviceMeasurementSeriesCsv");
async function loadAdminMeasurementSeriesPage(database, deviceId, query) {
  const points = await loadMeasurementSeriesForDevice(database, {
    deviceId,
    metric: query.metric,
    xAxis: query.xAxis,
    seqFrom: query.seqFrom,
    seqTo: query.seqTo,
    sampleTimeFrom: query.sampleTimeFrom,
    sampleTimeTo: query.sampleTimeTo,
    limit: query.limit + 1,
    cursor: query.cursor
  });
  const returnedPoints = points.slice(0, query.limit);
  const hasMore = points.length > query.limit;
  return {
    returnedPoints,
    hasMore,
    nextCursor: buildNextMeasurementSeriesCursor(
      returnedPoints,
      hasMore,
      query.xAxis
    )
  };
}
__name(loadAdminMeasurementSeriesPage, "loadAdminMeasurementSeriesPage");
function buildNextMeasurementCursor(measurements2, hasMore) {
  const lastMeasurement = measurements2.at(-1);
  if (!hasMore || lastMeasurement === void 0) {
    return null;
  }
  return encodeAdminMeasurementCursor({
    seq: lastMeasurement.seq,
    metric: lastMeasurement.metric,
    profile: lastMeasurement.profile
  });
}
__name(buildNextMeasurementCursor, "buildNextMeasurementCursor");
function buildNextMeasurementSeriesCursor(points, hasMore, xAxis) {
  const lastPoint = points.at(-1);
  if (!hasMore || lastPoint === void 0) {
    return null;
  }
  return encodeAdminMeasurementSeriesCursor({
    xAxis,
    seq: lastPoint.seq,
    sampleTime: lastPoint.sampleTime,
    profile: lastPoint.profile
  });
}
__name(buildNextMeasurementSeriesCursor, "buildNextMeasurementSeriesCursor");

// src/routes/admin/register.ts
function registerAdminRoutes(app2) {
  app2.get("/api/v1/admin/health", handleAdminHealth);
  app2.get("/api/v1/admin/devices", handleAdminDevicesOverview);
  app2.post("/api/v1/admin/devices", handleAdminDeviceCreate);
  app2.get("/api/v1/admin/devices/:deviceId", handleAdminDeviceInspection);
  app2.patch("/api/v1/admin/devices/:deviceId", handleAdminDeviceUpdate);
  app2.get("/api/v1/admin/devices/:deviceId/batches", handleAdminDeviceBatches);
  app2.get(
    "/api/v1/admin/devices/:deviceId/batches/:batchId",
    handleAdminDeviceBatchInspection
  );
  app2.get(
    "/api/v1/admin/devices/:deviceId/batches/:batchId/raw",
    handleAdminDeviceBatchRawPayload
  );
  app2.get(
    "/api/v1/admin/devices/:deviceId/measurements",
    handleAdminDeviceMeasurements
  );
  app2.get(
    "/api/v1/admin/devices/:deviceId/measurements/metrics",
    handleAdminDeviceMeasurementMetrics
  );
  app2.get(
    "/api/v1/admin/devices/:deviceId/measurements/series",
    handleAdminDeviceMeasurementSeries
  );
  app2.get(
    "/api/v1/admin/devices/:deviceId/measurements/series.csv",
    handleAdminDeviceMeasurementSeriesCsv
  );
}
__name(registerAdminRoutes, "registerAdminRoutes");

              </div>

            <div id="create-device-alert" class="alert alert-danger mt-3 mb-0 d-none" role="alert"></div>
            <div id="create-device-success" class="alert alert-success mt-3 mb-0 d-none" role="status"></div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </dialog>

      <dialog id="rotate-token-dialog" class="admin-dialog">
        <div class="card admin-dialog-card">
          <div class="card-header d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
            <span class="fw-semibold">Rotate token</span>
            <button id="rotate-token-close-button" class="btn btn-outline-secondary btn-sm admin-icon-button" type="button" aria-label="Close">x</button>
          </div>
          <div class="card-body">
            <form id="rotate-token-form" class="vstack gap-3">
              <div>
                <label class="form-label" for="rotate-token-device-id">Device id</label>
                <input id="rotate-token-device-id" class="form-control form-control-sm" type="text" disabled>
              </div>
              <div>
                <label class="form-label" for="rotate-token-value">New device token</label>
                <input id="rotate-token-value" class="form-control form-control-sm" type="password" minlength="16" maxlength="512" autocomplete="off" spellcheck="false" required>
              </div>
              <div class="alert alert-warning py-2 mb-0 small" role="status">Rotation immediately invalidates the previous device token.</div>
              <div class="d-flex justify-content-end gap-2">
                <button id="rotate-token-cancel-button" class="btn btn-outline-secondary btn-sm" type="button">Cancel</button>
                <button id="rotate-token-button" class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" type="submit">
                  <span id="rotate-token-spinner" class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm me-2 d-none" aria-hidden="true"></span>
                  Rotate
                </button>
              </div>
            </form>
            <div id="rotate-token-alert" class="alert alert-danger mt-3 mb-0 d-none" role="alert"></div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </dialog>

      <dialog id="edit-device-dialog" class="admin-dialog">
        <div class="card admin-dialog-card">
          <div class="card-header d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
            <span class="fw-semibold">Edit device</span>
            <button id="edit-device-close-button" class="btn btn-outline-secondary btn-sm admin-icon-button" type="button" aria-label="Close">x</button>
          </div>
          <div class="card-body">
            <form id="edit-device-form" class="vstack gap-3">
              <div>
                <label class="form-label" for="edit-device-id">Device id</label>
                <input id="edit-device-id" class="form-control form-control-sm" type="text" disabled>
              </div>
              <div>
                <label class="form-label" for="edit-device-display-name">Display name</label>
                <input id="edit-device-display-name" class="form-control form-control-sm" type="text" maxlength="128" autocomplete="off">
              </div>
              <div class="row g-2 align-items-end">
                <div class="col-7">
                  <label class="form-label" for="edit-device-config-revision">Config revision</label>
                  <input id="edit-device-config-revision" class="form-control form-control-sm" type="number" min="1" max="2147483647" step="1" required>
                </div>
                <div class="col-5 pb-1">
                  <div class="form-check">
                    <input id="edit-device-active" class="form-check-input" type="checkbox">
                    <label class="form-check-label" for="edit-device-active">Active</label>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div class="d-flex justify-content-end gap-2">
                <button id="edit-device-cancel-button" class="btn btn-outline-secondary btn-sm" type="button">Cancel</button>
                <button id="edit-device-button" class="btn btn-primary btn-sm" type="submit">
                  <span id="edit-device-spinner" class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm me-2 d-none" aria-hidden="true"></span>
                  Save
                </button>
              </div>
            </form>
            <div id="edit-device-alert" class="alert alert-danger mt-3 mb-0 d-none" role="alert"></div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </dialog>

      <dialog id="batch-detail-dialog" class="admin-dialog admin-dialog-wide">
        <div class="card admin-dialog-card">
          <div class="card-header d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
            <span id="batch-detail-title" class="fw-semibold">Batch detail</span>
            <button id="batch-detail-close-button" class="btn btn-outline-secondary btn-sm admin-icon-button" type="button" aria-label="Close">x</button>
          </div>
          <div id="batch-detail-body" class="card-body admin-detail small text-body-secondary">
            Select a batch.
          </div>
        </div>
      </dialog>
    </main>
  </body>
</html>
`;
var ADMIN_UI_STYLES = `:root {
