var ADMIN_UI_SCRIPT = `"use strict";

const ADMIN_HEADER = "X-TM-Admin-Token";
const SERIES_LIMIT = 1000;
const SVG_NS = "http://www.w3.org/2000/svg";

const state = {
  adminToken: null,
  authStatus: "anonymous",
  devices: [],
  selectedDeviceId: null,
  deviceDetail: null,
  batches: [],
  batchDetail: null,
  metrics: [],
  selectedMetric: null,
  xAxis: "seq",
  series: null,
  loading: {
    devices: false,
    device: false,
    batches: false,
    metrics: false,
    series: false,
    csv: false,
    rawBatch: false,
    deviceCreate: false,
    deviceEdit: false,
    deviceTokenRotate: false,
    batchDetail: false
  },
  errorMessage: null,
  loginError: null,
  createDeviceError: null,
  createDeviceSuccess: null,
  editDeviceError: null,
  rotateTokenError: null,
  batchDetailError: null,
  batchRawDownloadError: null
};

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", initializeAdminUi);

function initializeAdminUi() {
  byId("login-form").addEventListener("submit", handleLoginSubmit);
  byId("logout-button").addEventListener("click", function () {
    clearAuth();
  });
  byId("refresh-button").addEventListener("click", function () {
    void loadDevices();
  });
  byId("open-create-device-button").addEventListener("click", openCreateDeviceDialog);
  byId("create-device-close-button").addEventListener("click", closeCreateDeviceDialog);
  byId("create-device-cancel-button").addEventListener("click", closeCreateDeviceDialog);
  byId("create-device-dialog").addEventListener("click", function (event) {
    if (event.target === event.currentTarget && !state.loading.deviceCreate) {
      closeCreateDeviceDialog();
    }
  });
  byId("create-device-dialog").addEventListener("close", function () {
    clearCreateDeviceToken();
  });
  byId("create-device-form").addEventListener("submit", handleCreateDeviceSubmit);
  byId("open-edit-device-button").addEventListener("click", openEditDeviceDialog);
  byId("edit-device-close-button").addEventListener("click", closeEditDeviceDialog);
  byId("edit-device-cancel-button").addEventListener("click", closeEditDeviceDialog);
  byId("edit-device-dialog").addEventListener("click", function (event) {
    if (event.target === event.currentTarget && !state.loading.deviceEdit) {
      closeEditDeviceDialog();
    }
  });
  byId("edit-device-form").addEventListener("submit", handleEditDeviceSubmit);
  byId("open-rotate-token-button").addEventListener("click", openRotateTokenDialog);
  byId("rotate-token-close-button").addEventListener("click", closeRotateTokenDialog);
  byId("rotate-token-cancel-button").addEventListener("click", closeRotateTokenDialog);
  byId("rotate-token-dialog").addEventListener("click", function (event) {
    if (event.target === event.currentTarget && !state.loading.deviceTokenRotate) {
      closeRotateTokenDialog();
    }
  });
  byId("rotate-token-dialog").addEventListener("close", function () {
    clearRotateDeviceToken();
  });
  byId("rotate-token-form").addEventListener("submit", handleRotateTokenSubmit);
  byId("batch-detail-close-button").addEventListener("click", closeBatchDetailDialog);
  byId("batch-detail-dialog").addEventListener("click", function (event) {
    if (event.target === event.currentTarget && !state.loading.batchDetail) {
      closeBatchDetailDialog();
    }
  });
  byId("devices-table-body").addEventListener("click", function (event) {
    const target = event.target;
    if (!(target instanceof Element)) {
      return;
    }

    const button = target.closest("button[data-device-id]");
    if (button === null) {
      return;
    }

    const deviceId = button.getAttribute("data-device-id");
    if (deviceId !== null) {
      void selectDevice(deviceId);
    }
  });
  byId("batches-table-body").addEventListener("click", function (event) {
    const target = event.target;
    if (!(target instanceof Element)) {
      return;
    }

    const button = target.closest("button[data-batch-id]");
    if (button === null) {
      return;
    }

    const batchId = button.getAttribute("data-batch-id");
    if (batchId !== null) {
      void openBatchDetailDialog(batchId);
    }
  });
  byId("metric-select").addEventListener("change", function (event) {
    const target = event.target;
    if (target instanceof HTMLSelectElement) {
      state.selectedMetric = target.value || null;
      void loadSeries();
    }
  });
  byId("x-axis-seq").addEventListener("change", handleXAxisChange);
  byId("x-axis-sample-time").addEventListener("change", handleXAxisChange);
  byId("csv-button").addEventListener("click", function () {
    void downloadCsv();
  });

  renderAll();
}

async function handleLoginSubmit(event) {
  event.preventDefault();
  const tokenInput = byId("admin-token-input");
  const token = tokenInput.value.trim();

  if (token.length === 0) {
    state.loginError = "Enter an admin token.";
    renderAuth();
    return;
  }

  state.authStatus = "checking";
  state.loginError = null;
  renderAuth();

  try {
    await adminJson("/api/v1/admin/health", token);
    state.adminToken = token;
    tokenInput.value = "";
    state.authStatus = "authenticated";
    state.errorMessage = null;
    renderAll();
    await loadDevices();
  } catch (error) {
    state.adminToken = null;
    state.authStatus = "anonymous";
    state.loginError = formatError(error);
    renderAll();
  }
}

function handleXAxisChange(event) {
  const target = event.target;
  if (target instanceof HTMLInputElement && target.checked) {
    state.xAxis = target.value === "sample_time" ? "sample_time" : "seq";
    void loadSeries();
  }
}

function openCreateDeviceDialog() {
  const dialog = createDeviceDialog();
  state.createDeviceError = null;
  state.createDeviceSuccess = null;
  renderCreateDevice();

  if (!dialog.open) {
    dialog.showModal();
  }

  byId("create-device-id").focus();
}

function closeCreateDeviceDialog() {
  const dialog = createDeviceDialog();
  if (dialog.open) {
    dialog.close();
  }
}

function openEditDeviceDialog() {
  const device = state.deviceDetail;
  if (device === null) {
    return;
  }

  const dialog = editDeviceDialog();
  const deviceIdInput = byId("edit-device-id");
  const displayNameInput = byId("edit-device-display-name");
  const activeInput = byId("edit-device-active");
  const configRevisionInput = byId("edit-device-config-revision");

  if (
    !(deviceIdInput instanceof HTMLInputElement) ||
    !(displayNameInput instanceof HTMLInputElement) ||
    !(activeInput instanceof HTMLInputElement) ||
    !(configRevisionInput instanceof HTMLInputElement)
  ) {
    throw new Error("Edit-device form is not available.");
  }

  deviceIdInput.value = device.device_id;
  displayNameInput.value = device.display_name ?? "";
  activeInput.checked = Boolean(device.active);
  configRevisionInput.value = String(device.config_revision);
  state.editDeviceError = null;
  renderEditDevice();

  if (!dialog.open) {
    dialog.showModal();
  }

  displayNameInput.focus();
}

function closeEditDeviceDialog() {
  const dialog = editDeviceDialog();
  if (dialog.open) {
    dialog.close();
  }
}

function openRotateTokenDialog() {
  const device = state.deviceDetail;
  if (device === null) {
    return;
  }

  const dialog = rotateTokenDialog();
  const deviceIdInput = byId("rotate-token-device-id");
  const tokenInput = byId("rotate-token-value");

  if (
    !(deviceIdInput instanceof HTMLInputElement) ||
    !(tokenInput instanceof HTMLInputElement)
  ) {
    throw new Error("Rotate-token form is not available.");
  }

  deviceIdInput.value = device.device_id;
  tokenInput.value = "";
  state.rotateTokenError = null;
  renderRotateToken();

  if (!dialog.open) {
    dialog.showModal();
  }

  tokenInput.focus();
}

function closeRotateTokenDialog() {
  const dialog = rotateTokenDialog();
  if (dialog.open) {
    dialog.close();
  }
}

function closeBatchDetailDialog() {
  const dialog = batchDetailDialog();
  if (dialog.open) {
    dialog.close();
  }
}

async function handleCreateDeviceSubmit(event) {
  event.preventDefault();

  const token = requireToken();
  if (token === null) {
    return;
  }

  const form = byId("create-device-form");
  const deviceIdInput = byId("create-device-id");
  const deviceTokenInput = byId("create-device-token");
  const displayNameInput = byId("create-device-display-name");
  const activeInput = byId("create-device-active");
  const configRevisionInput = byId("create-device-config-revision");

  if (
    !(form instanceof HTMLFormElement) ||
    !(deviceIdInput instanceof HTMLInputElement) ||
    !(deviceTokenInput instanceof HTMLInputElement) ||
    !(displayNameInput instanceof HTMLInputElement) ||
    !(activeInput instanceof HTMLInputElement) ||
    !(configRevisionInput instanceof HTMLInputElement)
  ) {
    throw new Error("Create-device form is not available.");
  }

  if (!form.reportValidity()) {
    return;
  }

  const configRevision = Number(configRevisionInput.value);

  state.loading.deviceCreate = true;
  state.createDeviceError = null;
  state.createDeviceSuccess = null;
  renderCreateDevice();

  const displayName = displayNameInput.value.trim();
  const requestBody = {
    device_id: deviceIdInput.value.trim(),
    token: deviceTokenInput.value,
    display_name: displayName.length === 0 ? null : displayName,
    active: activeInput.checked,
    config_revision: Number.isFinite(configRevision) ? configRevision : 1
  };
  deviceTokenInput.value = "";

  try {
    const body = await adminJson("/api/v1/admin/devices", token, {
      method: "POST",
      jsonBody: requestBody
    });
    const createdDeviceId = body.device?.device_id ?? requestBody.device_id;

    form.reset();
    state.selectedDeviceId = createdDeviceId;
    state.createDeviceSuccess = "Created " + createdDeviceId + ".";
    await loadDevices();
    closeCreateDeviceDialog();
  } catch (error) {
    state.createDeviceError = formatError(error);
  } finally {
    deviceTokenInput.value = "";
    state.loading.deviceCreate = false;
    renderCreateDevice();
  }
}

async function handleEditDeviceSubmit(event) {
  event.preventDefault();

  const token = requireToken();
  const device = state.deviceDetail;
  if (token === null || device === null) {
    return;
  }

  const form = byId("edit-device-form");
  const displayNameInput = byId("edit-device-display-name");
  const activeInput = byId("edit-device-active");
  const configRevisionInput = byId("edit-device-config-revision");

  if (
    !(form instanceof HTMLFormElement) ||
    !(displayNameInput instanceof HTMLInputElement) ||
    !(activeInput instanceof HTMLInputElement) ||
    !(configRevisionInput instanceof HTMLInputElement)
  ) {
    throw new Error("Edit-device form is not available.");
  }

  if (!form.reportValidity()) {
    return;
  }

  const displayName = displayNameInput.value.trim();
  const configRevision = Number(configRevisionInput.value);
  const deviceId = device.device_id;

  state.loading.deviceEdit = true;
  state.editDeviceError = null;
  renderEditDevice();

  try {
    const body = await adminJson("/api/v1/admin/devices/" + encodeURIComponent(deviceId), token, {
      method: "PATCH",
      jsonBody: {
        display_name: displayName.length === 0 ? null : displayName,
        active: activeInput.checked,
        config_revision: Number.isFinite(configRevision) ? configRevision : device.config_revision
      }
    });

    if (state.selectedDeviceId === deviceId) {
      state.deviceDetail = body.device ?? state.deviceDetail;
    }

    await loadDevices();
    closeEditDeviceDialog();
  } catch (error) {
    state.editDeviceError = formatError(error);
  } finally {
    state.loading.deviceEdit = false;
    renderEditDevice();
  }
}

async function handleRotateTokenSubmit(event) {
  event.preventDefault();

  const token = requireToken();
  const device = state.deviceDetail;
  if (token === null || device === null) {
    return;
  }

  const form = byId("rotate-token-form");
  const tokenInput = byId("rotate-token-value");

  if (
    !(form instanceof HTMLFormElement) ||
    !(tokenInput instanceof HTMLInputElement)
  ) {
    throw new Error("Rotate-token form is not available.");
  }

  if (!form.reportValidity()) {
    return;
  }

  const deviceId = device.device_id;
  const requestBody = {
    token: tokenInput.value
  };
  tokenInput.value = "";

  state.loading.deviceTokenRotate = true;
  state.rotateTokenError = null;
  renderRotateToken();

  try {
    const body = await adminJson("/api/v1/admin/devices/" + encodeURIComponent(deviceId), token, {
      method: "PATCH",
      jsonBody: requestBody
    });

    if (state.selectedDeviceId === deviceId) {
      state.deviceDetail = body.device ?? state.deviceDetail;
    }

    await loadDevices();
    closeRotateTokenDialog();
  } catch (error) {
    state.rotateTokenError = formatError(error);
  } finally {
    tokenInput.value = "";
    state.loading.deviceTokenRotate = false;
    renderRotateToken();
  }
}

async function openBatchDetailDialog(batchId) {
  const token = requireToken();
  const deviceId = state.selectedDeviceId;
  if (token === null || deviceId === null) {
    return;
  }

  const dialog = batchDetailDialog();
  state.batchDetail = null;
  state.batchDetailError = null;
  state.batchRawDownloadError = null;
  state.loading.batchDetail = true;
  renderBatchDetail();

  if (!dialog.open) {
    dialog.showModal();
  }

  try {
    const path =
      "/api/v1/admin/devices/" +
      encodeURIComponent(deviceId) +
      "/batches/" +
      encodeURIComponent(batchId);
    const body = await adminJson(path, token);

    if (state.selectedDeviceId === deviceId) {
      state.batchDetail = body.batch ?? null;
    }
  } catch (error) {
    state.batchDetailError = formatError(error);
  } finally {
    state.loading.batchDetail = false;
    renderBatchDetail();
  }
}

async function loadDevices() {
  const token = requireToken();
  if (token === null) {
    return;
  }

  state.loading.devices = true;
  state.errorMessage = null;
  renderDevices();
  renderGlobalAlert();

  try {
    const body = await adminJson("/api/v1/admin/devices", token);
    state.devices = Array.isArray(body.devices) ? body.devices : [];

    const selectedStillExists = state.devices.some(function (device) {
      return device.device_id === state.selectedDeviceId;
    });
    state.selectedDeviceId = selectedStillExists
      ? state.selectedDeviceId
      : state.devices[0]?.device_id ?? null;
  } catch (error) {
    handleApiError(error);
  } finally {
    state.loading.devices = false;
    renderDevices();
  }

  await loadSelectedDevice();
}

async function selectDevice(deviceId) {
  if (state.selectedDeviceId === deviceId) {
    return;
  }

  state.selectedDeviceId = deviceId;
  state.deviceDetail = null;
  state.batches = [];
  state.batchDetail = null;
  state.batchDetailError = null;
  state.batchRawDownloadError = null;
  state.metrics = [];
  state.selectedMetric = null;
  state.series = null;
  closeBatchDetailDialog();
  renderAll();
  await loadSelectedDevice();
}

async function loadSelectedDevice() {
  const token = requireToken();
  if (token === null) {
    return;
  }

  const deviceId = state.selectedDeviceId;
  if (deviceId === null) {
    state.deviceDetail = null;
    state.batches = [];
    state.batchDetail = null;
    state.batchDetailError = null;
    state.batchRawDownloadError = null;
    state.metrics = [];
    state.selectedMetric = null;
    state.series = null;
    renderAll();
    return;
  }

  state.loading.device = true;
  state.loading.batches = true;
  state.loading.metrics = true;
  state.errorMessage = null;
  renderDeviceDetail();
  renderEditDevice();
  renderRotateToken();
  renderBatches();
  renderMetrics();
  renderGlobalAlert();

  try {
    const pathDeviceId = encodeURIComponent(deviceId);
    const results = await Promise.all([
      adminJson("/api/v1/admin/devices/" + pathDeviceId, token),
      adminJson("/api/v1/admin/devices/" + pathDeviceId + "/batches", token),
      adminJson("/api/v1/admin/devices/" + pathDeviceId + "/measurements/metrics", token)
    ]);

    if (state.selectedDeviceId !== deviceId) {
      return;
    }

    state.deviceDetail = results[0].device ?? null;
    state.batches = Array.isArray(results[1].batches) ? results[1].batches : [];
    state.metrics = Array.isArray(results[2].metrics) ? results[2].metrics : [];

    const selectedMetricStillExists = state.metrics.some(function (metric) {
      return metric.metric === state.selectedMetric;
    });
    state.selectedMetric = selectedMetricStillExists
      ? state.selectedMetric
      : state.metrics[0]?.metric ?? null;
  } catch (error) {
    handleApiError(error);
  } finally {
    state.loading.device = false;
    state.loading.batches = false;
    state.loading.metrics = false;
    renderDeviceDetail();
    renderEditDevice();
    renderRotateToken();
    renderBatches();
    renderMetrics();
  }

  await loadSeries();
}

async function loadSeries() {
  const token = requireToken();
  if (token === null) {
    return;
  }

  const deviceId = state.selectedDeviceId;
  const metricSummary = selectedMetricSummary();
  if (deviceId === null || metricSummary === null) {
    state.series = null;
    renderSeries();
    return;
  }

  state.loading.series = true;
  state.errorMessage = null;
  renderSeries();
  renderGlobalAlert();

  try {
    const params = buildSeriesParams(metricSummary, state.xAxis);
    const path =
      "/api/v1/admin/devices/" +
      encodeURIComponent(deviceId) +
      "/measurements/series?" +
      params.toString();
    const series = await adminJson(path, token);

    if (
      state.selectedDeviceId === deviceId &&
      state.selectedMetric === metricSummary.metric
    ) {
      state.series = series;
    }
  } catch (error) {
    state.series = null;
    handleApiError(error);
  } finally {
    state.loading.series = false;
    renderSeries();
  }
}

async function downloadCsv() {
  const token = requireToken();
  const deviceId = state.selectedDeviceId;
  const metricSummary = selectedMetricSummary();
  if (token === null || deviceId === null || metricSummary === null) {
    return;
  }

  state.loading.csv = true;
  state.errorMessage = null;
  renderMetrics();
  renderGlobalAlert();

  try {
    const params = buildSeriesParams(metricSummary, state.xAxis);
    const path =
      "/api/v1/admin/devices/" +
      encodeURIComponent(deviceId) +
      "/measurements/series.csv?" +
      params.toString();
    const csv = await adminCsv(path, token);
    triggerDownload(csv.blob, csv.filename);

    if (csv.hasMore) {
      state.errorMessage =
        "CSV export is bounded to the displayed metric window. Narrow the range through a future UI batch if more rows are needed.";
    }
  } catch (error) {
    handleApiError(error);
  } finally {
    state.loading.csv = false;
    renderMetrics();
    renderGlobalAlert();
  }
}

async function downloadRawBatch() {
  const token = requireToken();
  const batch = state.batchDetail;
  const deviceId = state.selectedDeviceId;
  if (token === null || batch === null || deviceId === null) {
    return;
  }

  state.loading.rawBatch = true;
  state.batchRawDownloadError = null;
  renderBatchDetail();

  try {
    const path =
      "/api/v1/admin/devices/" +
      encodeURIComponent(deviceId) +
      "/batches/" +
      encodeURIComponent(batch.batch_id) +
      "/raw";
    const rawPayload = await adminBlob(
      path,
      token,
      fallbackRawBatchFilename(batch)
    );
    triggerDownload(rawPayload.blob, rawPayload.filename);
  } catch (error) {
    state.batchRawDownloadError = formatError(error);
  } finally {
    state.loading.rawBatch = false;
    renderBatchDetail();
  }
}

async function adminJson(path, token, options = {}) {
  const headers = buildAdminHeaders(token);
  const fetchOptions = {
    method: options.method ?? "GET",
    cache: "no-store",
    headers
  };

  if (options.jsonBody !== undefined) {
    headers.set("Content-Type", "application/json");
    fetchOptions.body = JSON.stringify(options.jsonBody);
  }

  const response = await fetch(path, {
    ...fetchOptions
  });
  const body = await response.json().catch(function () {
    return null;
  });

  if (!response.ok) {
    if (response.status === 401 && state.adminToken !== null) {
      clearAuth("Admin token was rejected. Enter it again.");
    }

    throw new Error(adminErrorMessage(response.status, body));
  }

  return body ?? {};
}

async function adminCsv(path, token) {
  const download = await adminBlob(path, token, fallbackCsvFilename());

  return {
    blob: download.blob,
    filename: download.filename,
    hasMore: download.headers.get("X-TM-Has-More") === "true"
  };
}

async function adminBlob(path, token, fallbackFilename) {
  const response = await fetch(path, {
    cache: "no-store",
    headers: buildAdminHeaders(token)
  });

  if (!response.ok) {
    const body = await response.json().catch(function () {
      return null;
    });

    if (response.status === 401 && state.adminToken !== null) {
      clearAuth("Admin token was rejected. Enter it again.");
    }

    throw new Error(adminErrorMessage(response.status, body));
  }

  return {
    blob: await response.blob(),
    filename:
      filenameFromContentDisposition(response.headers.get("Content-Disposition")) ??
      fallbackFilename,
    headers: response.headers
  };
}

function buildAdminHeaders(token) {
  const headers = new Headers();
  headers.set(ADMIN_HEADER, token);
  return headers;
}

function adminErrorMessage(status, body) {
  if (body !== null && typeof body.reason === "string") {
    return "Request failed: " + body.reason + " (" + status + ").";
  }

  if (body !== null && body.status === "not_found") {
    return "Requested admin resource was not found (" + status + ").";
  }

  return "Request failed with HTTP " + status + ".";
}

function clearAuth(message) {
  state.adminToken = null;
  state.authStatus = "anonymous";
  state.devices = [];
  state.selectedDeviceId = null;
  state.deviceDetail = null;
  state.batches = [];
  state.batchDetail = null;
  state.metrics = [];
  state.selectedMetric = null;
  state.series = null;
  state.errorMessage = null;
  state.loginError = message ?? null;
  state.createDeviceError = null;
  state.createDeviceSuccess = null;
  state.editDeviceError = null;
  state.rotateTokenError = null;
  state.batchDetailError = null;
  state.batchRawDownloadError = null;
  closeCreateDeviceDialog();
  closeEditDeviceDialog();
  closeRotateTokenDialog();
  closeBatchDetailDialog();
  renderAll();
}

function requireToken() {
  if (state.adminToken === null) {
    return null;
  }

  return state.adminToken;
}

function handleApiError(error) {
  if (state.authStatus === "authenticated") {
    state.errorMessage = formatError(error);
    renderGlobalAlert();
  }
}

function formatError(error) {
  return error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Request failed.";
}

function buildSeriesParams(metricSummary, xAxis) {
  const params = new URLSearchParams();
  params.set("metric", metricSummary.metric);
  params.set("x_axis", xAxis);
  params.set("limit", String(SERIES_LIMIT));
  params.set("seq_from", String(Math.max(metricSummary.first_seq, metricSummary.last_seq - (SERIES_LIMIT - 1))));
  params.set("seq_to", String(metricSummary.last_seq));
  return params;
}

function selectedMetricSummary() {
  if (state.selectedMetric === null) {
    return null;
  }

  return (
    state.metrics.find(function (metric) {
      return metric.metric === state.selectedMetric;
    }) ?? null
  );
}

function renderAll() {
  renderAuth();
  renderGlobalAlert();
  renderCreateDevice();
  renderEditDevice();
  renderRotateToken();
  renderDevices();
  renderDeviceDetail();
  renderBatches();
  renderBatchDetail();
  renderMetrics();
  renderSeries();
}

function renderAuth() {
  const authenticated = state.authStatus === "authenticated";
  byId("login-section").classList.toggle("d-none", authenticated);
  byId("dashboard-section").classList.toggle("d-none", !authenticated);
  byId("logout-button").classList.toggle("d-none", !authenticated);
  setText("auth-status", authenticated ? "Signed in" : "Signed out");
  byId("auth-status").className = authenticated
    ? "badge text-bg-success"
    : "badge text-bg-secondary";

  const checking = state.authStatus === "checking";
  byId("login-button").disabled = checking;
  byId("login-spinner").classList.toggle("d-none", !checking);
  const loginAlert = byId("login-alert");
  loginAlert.classList.toggle("d-none", state.loginError === null);
  loginAlert.textContent = state.loginError ?? "";
}

function renderGlobalAlert() {
  const alert = byId("global-alert");
  alert.classList.toggle("d-none", state.errorMessage === null);
  alert.textContent = state.errorMessage ?? "";
}

function renderCreateDevice() {
  const createButton = byId("create-device-button");
  const spinner = byId("create-device-spinner");
  const errorAlert = byId("create-device-alert");
  const successAlert = byId("create-device-success");

  createButton.disabled = state.loading.deviceCreate;
  spinner.classList.toggle("d-none", !state.loading.deviceCreate);

  errorAlert.classList.toggle("d-none", state.createDeviceError === null);
  errorAlert.textContent = state.createDeviceError ?? "";

  successAlert.classList.toggle("d-none", state.createDeviceSuccess === null);
  successAlert.textContent = state.createDeviceSuccess ?? "";
}

function renderEditDevice() {
  const openButton = byId("open-edit-device-button");
  const saveButton = byId("edit-device-button");
  const spinner = byId("edit-device-spinner");
  const errorAlert = byId("edit-device-alert");
  const canEdit =
    state.authStatus === "authenticated" &&
    state.deviceDetail !== null &&
    !state.loading.device &&
    !state.loading.deviceEdit;

  openButton.disabled = !canEdit;
  saveButton.disabled = state.loading.deviceEdit;
  spinner.classList.toggle("d-none", !state.loading.deviceEdit);

  errorAlert.classList.toggle("d-none", state.editDeviceError === null);
  errorAlert.textContent = state.editDeviceError ?? "";
}

function renderRotateToken() {
  const openButton = byId("open-rotate-token-button");
  const rotateButton = byId("rotate-token-button");
  const spinner = byId("rotate-token-spinner");
  const errorAlert = byId("rotate-token-alert");
  const canRotate =
    state.authStatus === "authenticated" &&
    state.deviceDetail !== null &&
    !state.loading.device &&
    !state.loading.deviceTokenRotate;

  openButton.disabled = !canRotate;
  rotateButton.disabled = state.loading.deviceTokenRotate;
  spinner.classList.toggle("d-none", !state.loading.deviceTokenRotate);

  errorAlert.classList.toggle("d-none", state.rotateTokenError === null);
  errorAlert.textContent = state.rotateTokenError ?? "";
}

function renderDevices() {
  setText("device-count", state.loading.devices ? "..." : String(state.devices.length));
  const body = byId("devices-table-body");
  body.replaceChildren();

  for (const device of state.devices) {
    const row = document.createElement("tr");
    if (device.device_id === state.selectedDeviceId) {
      row.classList.add("table-primary");
    }

    const deviceCell = document.createElement("td");
    const button = document.createElement("button");
    button.type = "button";
    button.className = "btn btn-link btn-sm p-0 text-start admin-device-button";
    button.setAttribute("data-device-id", device.device_id);
    button.textContent = displayDeviceName(device);
    deviceCell.append(button);

    const activeCell = document.createElement("td");
    activeCell.append(statusBadge(device.active ? "Active" : "Inactive", device.active ? "success" : "secondary"));

    const seqCell = document.createElement("td");
    seqCell.textContent = nullableText(device.last_seq_accepted);

    row.append(deviceCell, activeCell, seqCell);
    body.append(row);
  }

  const empty = byId("devices-empty");
  empty.classList.toggle("d-none", state.loading.devices || state.devices.length > 0);
  empty.textContent = state.loading.devices ? "Loading devices..." : "No devices found.";
}

function renderDeviceDetail() {
  const detail = byId("device-detail");
  detail.replaceChildren();

  if (state.loading.device) {
    detail.textContent = "Loading device state...";
    return;
  }

  const device = state.deviceDetail;
  if (device === null) {
    detail.textContent = state.selectedDeviceId === null ? "Select a device." : "No device detail loaded.";
    return;
  }

  const list = document.createElement("dl");
  list.className = "row";
  appendDetail(list, "Device id", device.device_id);
  appendDetail(list, "Display name", device.display_name ?? "None");
  appendDetail(list, "Active", device.active ? "Yes" : "No");
  appendDetail(list, "Config revision", String(device.config_revision));
  appendDetail(list, "Created", formatUnixSeconds(device.created_at));
  appendDetail(list, "Last seen", formatUnixSeconds(device.last_seen_at));
  appendDetail(list, "Last accepted seq", nullableText(device.last_seq_accepted));
  detail.append(list);
}

function renderBatches() {
  setText("batch-count", state.loading.batches ? "..." : String(state.batches.length));
  const body = byId("batches-table-body");
  body.replaceChildren();

  for (const batch of state.batches) {
    const row = document.createElement("tr");

    const batchCell = document.createElement("td");
    batchCell.className = "admin-batch-id";
    batchCell.textContent = batch.batch_id;

    const seqCell = document.createElement("td");
    seqCell.textContent = String(batch.seq_first) + "-" + String(batch.seq_last);

    const receivedCell = document.createElement("td");
    receivedCell.textContent = formatUnixSeconds(batch.received_at);

    const statusCell = document.createElement("td");
    statusCell.append(statusBadge(batch.status, batchStatusTone(batch.status)));

    const detailCell = document.createElement("td");
    detailCell.className = "text-end";
    const detailButton = document.createElement("button");
    detailButton.type = "button";
    detailButton.className = "btn btn-outline-secondary btn-sm admin-icon-button";
    detailButton.setAttribute("data-batch-id", batch.batch_id);
    detailButton.setAttribute("aria-label", "Inspect batch " + batch.batch_id);
    detailButton.title = "Inspect batch";
    detailButton.textContent = String.fromCharCode(8981);
    detailCell.append(detailButton);

    row.append(batchCell, seqCell, receivedCell, statusCell, detailCell);
    body.append(row);
  }

  const empty = byId("batches-empty");
  empty.classList.toggle("d-none", state.loading.batches || state.batches.length > 0);
  empty.textContent = state.loading.batches ? "Loading batches..." : "No recent accepted batches found.";
}

function renderBatchDetail() {
  const body = byId("batch-detail-body");
  body.replaceChildren();
  setText("batch-detail-title", "Batch detail");

  if (state.loading.batchDetail) {
    body.textContent = "Loading batch detail...";
    return;
  }

  if (state.batchDetailError !== null) {
    const alert = document.createElement("div");
    alert.className = "alert alert-danger mb-0";
    alert.setAttribute("role", "alert");
    alert.textContent = state.batchDetailError;
    body.append(alert);
    return;
  }

  const batch = state.batchDetail;
  if (batch === null) {
    body.textContent = "Select a batch.";
    return;
  }

  const list = document.createElement("dl");
  list.className = "row";
  appendDetail(list, "Batch id", batch.batch_id);
  appendDetail(list, "Profile", batch.profile);
  appendDetail(list, "Seq range", String(batch.seq_first) + "-" + String(batch.seq_last));
  appendDetail(list, "Received", formatUnixSeconds(batch.received_at));
  appendDetailNode(list, "Status", statusBadge(batch.status, batchStatusTone(batch.status)));
  appendDetail(list, "R2 key", batch.raw_r2_key);
  appendDetail(list, "Payload SHA-256", batch.raw_payload_sha256);
  body.append(list);

  const actions = document.createElement("div");
  actions.className = "d-flex justify-content-end mb-3";
  const downloadButton = document.createElement("button");
  downloadButton.type = "button";
  downloadButton.className = "btn btn-outline-secondary btn-sm";
  downloadButton.disabled = state.loading.rawBatch;
  downloadButton.textContent = state.loading.rawBatch
    ? "Downloading..."
    : "Download raw JSON";
  downloadButton.addEventListener("click", function () {
    void downloadRawBatch();
  });
  actions.append(downloadButton);
  body.append(actions);

  if (state.batchRawDownloadError !== null) {
    const alert = document.createElement("div");
    alert.className = "alert alert-danger";
    alert.setAttribute("role", "alert");
    alert.textContent = state.batchRawDownloadError;
    body.append(alert);
  }

  const summary = batch.measurement_summary;
  const heading = document.createElement("h2");
  heading.className = "h6 mt-3 mb-2 text-body";
  heading.textContent = "Measurement summary";
  body.append(heading);

  const total = document.createElement("div");
  total.className = "mb-2";
  total.textContent =
    "Total expanded measurements: " +
    nullableText(summary?.total_count);
  body.append(total);

  const table = document.createElement("table");
  table.className = "table table-sm align-middle mb-0";
  const tableHead = document.createElement("thead");
  const headRow = document.createElement("tr");
  const familyHead = document.createElement("th");
  familyHead.scope = "col";
  familyHead.textContent = "Family";
  const countHead = document.createElement("th");
  countHead.scope = "col";
  countHead.className = "text-end";
  countHead.textContent = "Count";
  headRow.append(familyHead, countHead);
  tableHead.append(headRow);

  const tableBody = document.createElement("tbody");
  const byFamily = summary?.by_family ?? {};
  for (const family of ["vibwire", "shzk", "env", "power", "other"]) {
    const row = document.createElement("tr");
    const familyCell = document.createElement("td");
    familyCell.textContent = family;
    const countCell = document.createElement("td");
    countCell.className = "text-end";
    countCell.textContent = nullableText(byFamily[family]);
    row.append(familyCell, countCell);
    tableBody.append(row);
  }

  table.append(tableHead, tableBody);
  body.append(table);
}

function renderMetrics() {
  const select = byId("metric-select");
  select.replaceChildren();
  select.disabled = state.loading.metrics || state.metrics.length === 0;

  for (const metric of state.metrics) {
    const option = document.createElement("option");
    option.value = metric.metric;
    option.textContent = metric.metric + (metric.unit ? " (" + metric.unit + ")" : "");
    option.selected = metric.metric === state.selectedMetric;
    select.append(option);
  }

  const metricSummary = selectedMetricSummary();
  const meta = byId("metric-meta");
  if (state.loading.metrics) {
    meta.textContent = "Loading metrics...";
  } else if (metricSummary === null) {
    meta.textContent = "No metrics are available for the selected device.";
  } else {
    meta.textContent =
      String(state.metrics.length) +
      " metrics present. Selected " +
      metricSummary.metric +
      ", " +
      String(metricSummary.sample_count) +
      " samples, seq " +
      String(metricSummary.first_seq) +
      "-" +
      String(metricSummary.last_seq) +
      ".";
  }

  byId("x-axis-seq").disabled = metricSummary === null;
  byId("x-axis-sample-time").disabled = metricSummary === null;
  byId("x-axis-seq").checked = state.xAxis === "seq";
  byId("x-axis-sample-time").checked = state.xAxis === "sample_time";
  byId("csv-button").disabled = metricSummary === null || state.loading.csv || state.loading.series;
  byId("csv-button").textContent = state.loading.csv ? "Preparing CSV..." : "Download CSV";
}

function renderSeries() {
  const empty = byId("series-empty");
  const meta = byId("series-meta");

  if (state.loading.series) {
    empty.textContent = "Loading series...";
    meta.textContent = "";
    drawChart(null);
    return;
  }

  if (state.series === null) {
    empty.textContent = state.selectedMetric === null ? "No metric selected." : "No series loaded.";
    meta.textContent = "";
    drawChart(null);
    return;
  }

  empty.textContent =
    state.series.returned_count === 0 ? "No points returned for the selected metric window." : "";
  meta.textContent =
    String(state.series.returned_count) +
    " points returned" +
    (state.series.unit ? " in " + state.series.unit : "") +
    (state.series.has_more ? ". More points exist beyond this bounded result." : ".");
  drawChart(state.series);
}

function drawChart(series) {
  const svg = byId("series-chart");
  svg.replaceChildren();

  const title = svgElement("title");
  title.textContent = "Metric series chart";
  svg.append(title);

  const width = 800;
  const height = 260;
  const left = 56;
  const right = 20;
  const top = 20;
  const bottom = 42;
  const plotWidth = width - left - right;
  const plotHeight = height - top - bottom;

  if (series === null) {
    drawEmptyChart(svg, width, height, "No data");
    return;
  }

  const points = series.points
    .map(function (point) {
      const x = series.x_axis === "sample_time" ? point.sample_time : point.seq;
      const y = point.value;
      if (x === null || y === null || !Number.isFinite(x) || !Number.isFinite(y)) {
        return null;
      }

      return { x: x, y: y, seq: point.seq, sampleTime: point.sample_time };
    })
    .filter(function (point) {
      return point !== null;
    });

  if (points.length === 0) {
    drawEmptyChart(svg, width, height, "No numeric points");
    return;
  }

  const xValues = points.map(function (point) {
    return point.x;
  });
  const yValues = points.map(function (point) {
    return point.y;
  });
  const xMin = Math.min.apply(null, xValues);
  const xMax = Math.max.apply(null, xValues);
  const yMin = Math.min.apply(null, yValues);
  const yMax = Math.max.apply(null, yValues);
  const xRange = xMax === xMin ? 1 : xMax - xMin;
  const yRange = yMax === yMin ? 1 : yMax - yMin;

  function plotX(value) {
    return left + ((value - xMin) / xRange) * plotWidth;
  }

  function plotY(value) {
    return top + plotHeight - ((value - yMin) / yRange) * plotHeight;
  }

  drawLine(svg, left, top, left, top + plotHeight, "chart-axis");
  drawLine(svg, left, top + plotHeight, width - right, top + plotHeight, "chart-axis");
  drawLine(svg, left, top, width - right, top, "chart-grid");
  drawLine(svg, width - right, top, width - right, top + plotHeight, "chart-grid");
  drawText(svg, left - 8, top + 4, formatNumber(yMax), "chart-label", "end");
  drawText(svg, left - 8, top + plotHeight, formatNumber(yMin), "chart-label", "end");
  drawText(svg, left, height - 12, formatAxisValue(xMin, series.x_axis), "chart-label", "start");
  drawText(svg, width - right, height - 12, formatAxisValue(xMax, series.x_axis), "chart-label", "end");

  const line = svgElement("polyline");
  line.setAttribute(
    "points",
    points
      .map(function (point) {
        return formatNumber(plotX(point.x)) + "," + formatNumber(plotY(point.y));
      })
      .join(" ")
  );
  line.setAttribute("class", "chart-line");
  svg.append(line);

  const circleLimit = Math.min(points.length, 200);
  for (let index = 0; index < circleLimit; index += 1) {
    const point = points[index];
    const circle = svgElement("circle");
    circle.setAttribute("class", "chart-point");
    circle.setAttribute("cx", formatNumber(plotX(point.x)));
    circle.setAttribute("cy", formatNumber(plotY(point.y)));
    circle.setAttribute("r", points.length === 1 ? "5" : "3");

    const pointTitle = svgElement("title");
    pointTitle.textContent =
      "seq " +
      String(point.seq) +
      ", sample time " +
      formatUnixSeconds(point.sampleTime) +
      ", value " +
      formatNumber(point.y);
    circle.append(pointTitle);
    svg.append(circle);
  }
}

function drawEmptyChart(svg, width, height, label) {
  drawLine(svg, 56, 218, width - 20, 218, "chart-axis");
  drawText(svg, width / 2, height / 2, label, "chart-empty-label", "middle");
}

function drawLine(svg, x1, y1, x2, y2, className) {
  const line = svgElement("line");
  line.setAttribute("x1", formatNumber(x1));
  line.setAttribute("y1", formatNumber(y1));
  line.setAttribute("x2", formatNumber(x2));
  line.setAttribute("y2", formatNumber(y2));
  line.setAttribute("class", className);
  svg.append(line);
}

function drawText(svg, x, y, value, className, anchor) {
  const text = svgElement("text");
  text.setAttribute("x", formatNumber(x));
  text.setAttribute("y", formatNumber(y));
  text.setAttribute("class", className);
  text.setAttribute("text-anchor", anchor);
  text.textContent = value;
  svg.append(text);
}

function svgElement(name) {
  return document.createElementNS(SVG_NS, name);
}

function appendDetail(list, label, value) {
  appendDetailNode(list, label, document.createTextNode(value));
}

function appendDetailNode(list, label, valueNode) {
  const term = document.createElement("dt");
  term.className = "col-5";
  term.textContent = label;

  const description = document.createElement("dd");
  description.className = "col-7";
  description.append(valueNode);

  list.append(term, description);
}

function statusBadge(label, tone) {
  const badge = document.createElement("span");
  badge.className = "badge text-bg-" + tone;
  badge.textContent = label;
  return badge;
}

function batchStatusTone(status) {
  if (status === "accepted") {
    return "success";
  }

  if (status === "failed") {
    return "danger";
  }

  return "secondary";
}

function displayDeviceName(device) {
  if (device.display_name) {
    return device.display_name + " (" + device.device_id + ")";
  }

  return device.device_id;
}

function formatUnixSeconds(value) {
  if (value === null || value === undefined) {
    return "None";
  }

  return new Date(value * 1000).toLocaleString();
}

function nullableText(value) {
  return value === null || value === undefined ? "None" : String(value);
}

function formatAxisValue(value, xAxis) {
  if (xAxis === "sample_time") {
    return new Date(value * 1000).toLocaleString(undefined, {
      month: "short",
      day: "numeric",
      hour: "2-digit",
      minute: "2-digit"
    });
  }

  return formatNumber(value);
}

function formatNumber(value) {
  if (Math.abs(value) >= 1000) {
    return String(Math.round(value));
  }

  return Number(value.toFixed(3)).toString();
}

function filenameFromContentDisposition(value) {
  if (value === null) {
    return null;
  }

  const parts = value.split(";");
  for (const part of parts) {
    const trimmed = part.trim();
    if (trimmed.toLowerCase().startsWith("filename=")) {
      return trimmed.slice("filename=".length).replace(/^"|"$/g, "");
    }
  }

  return null;
}

function fallbackCsvFilename() {
  const deviceId = state.selectedDeviceId ?? "device";
  const metric = state.selectedMetric ?? "metric";
  return "tunnel-monitor-" + deviceId + "-" + metric + ".csv";
}

function fallbackRawBatchFilename(batch) {
  return (
    "tunnel-monitor-" +
    safeDownloadSegment(batch.device_id) +
    "-" +
    safeDownloadSegment(batch.batch_id) +
    ".json"
  );
}

function safeDownloadSegment(value) {
  const segment = String(value).replace(/[^A-Za-z0-9._-]+/g, "_");
  return segment.length > 0 ? segment : "unknown";
}

function triggerDownload(blob, filename) {
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const link = document.createElement("a");
  link.href = url;
  link.download = filename;
  document.body.append(link);
  link.click();
  link.remove();
  window.setTimeout(function () {
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  }, 0);
}

function createDeviceDialog() {
  const dialog = byId("create-device-dialog");
  if (!(dialog instanceof HTMLDialogElement)) {
    throw new Error("Create-device dialog is not available.");
  }

  return dialog;
}

function editDeviceDialog() {
  const dialog = byId("edit-device-dialog");
  if (!(dialog instanceof HTMLDialogElement)) {
    throw new Error("Edit-device dialog is not available.");
  }

  return dialog;
}

  }

  return dialog;
}

function batchDetailDialog() {
  const dialog = byId("batch-detail-dialog");
  if (!(dialog instanceof HTMLDialogElement)) {
    throw new Error("Batch-detail dialog is not available.");
  }

}

function clearCreateDeviceToken() {
  const tokenInput = byId("create-device-token");
  if (tokenInput instanceof HTMLInputElement) {
    tokenInput.value = "";
  }
}

function clearRotateDeviceToken() {
  const tokenInput = byId("rotate-token-value");
  if (tokenInput instanceof HTMLInputElement) {
    tokenInput.value = "";
  }
}

function byId(id) {
  const element = document.getElementById(id);
  if (element === null) {
    throw new Error("Missing UI element: " + id);
  }

  return element;
}

function setText(id, value) {
  byId(id).textContent = value;
}

var ADMIN_UI_CONTENT_SECURITY_POLICY = [
  "default-src 'none'",

  "object-src 'none'",

  "style-src 'self' https://cdn.jsdelivr.net"

function uiHeaders(contentType, options = {}) {
  const headers = new Headers({
    "Content-Type": contentType,
    "Referrer-Policy": "no-referrer",
    "X-Content-Type-Options": "nosniff"
  });
  if (options.contentSecurityPolicy !== void 0) {
    headers.set("Content-Security-Policy", options.contentSecurityPolicy);
  }
  return headers;
}

// src/domain/measurements.ts
var ENVIRONMENT_MEASUREMENTS = [
  { field: "t_c", metric: "env.temperature", unit: "degC" },
  { field: "rh_pct", metric: "env.relative_humidity", unit: "pct" },
  { field: "p_pa", metric: "env.pressure", unit: "Pa" }
];
var POWER_MEASUREMENTS = [
  { field: "vin_v", metric: "power.input_voltage", unit: "V" },
  { field: "iin_a", metric: "power.input_current", unit: "A" }
];
function expandTmBatchV1ToMeasurements(batch) {
  return batch.samples.flatMap((sample) => {
    return expandSampleToMeasurements(batch, sample);
  });
}
__name(expandTmBatchV1ToMeasurements, "expandTmBatchV1ToMeasurements");
function expandSampleToMeasurements(batch, sample) {
  const measurements2 = [];
  for (const [index2, value] of sample.vw_f.entries()) {
    measurements2.push(
      createMeasurement(
        batch,
        sample,
        `vibwire.${channelName(index2)}.frequency`,
        value,
        "Hz"
      )
    );
  }
  for (const [index2, value] of sample.vw_t.entries()) {
    measurements2.push(
      createMeasurement(
        batch,
        sample,
        `vibwire.${channelName(index2)}.temperature`,
        value,
        "degC"
      )
    );
  }
  for (const [index2, value] of sample.shzk_t.entries()) {
    measurements2.push(
      createMeasurement(
        batch,
        sample,
        `shzk.${channelName(index2)}.temperature`,
        value,
        "degC"
      )
    );
  }
  for (const measurement of ENVIRONMENT_MEASUREMENTS) {
    measurements2.push(
      createMeasurement(
        batch,
        sample,
        measurement.metric,
        sample.env[measurement.field],
        measurement.unit
      )
    );
  }
  for (const measurement of POWER_MEASUREMENTS) {
    measurements2.push(
      createMeasurement(
        batch,
        sample,
        measurement.metric,
        sample.pwr[measurement.field],
        measurement.unit
      )
    );
  }
  return measurements2;
}
__name(expandSampleToMeasurements, "expandSampleToMeasurements");
function createMeasurement(batch, sample, metric, value, unit) {
  return {
    deviceId: batch.device_id,
    profile: batch.profile,
    seq: sample.seq,
    t: sample.t,
    metric,
    value,
    unit
  };
}
__name(createMeasurement, "createMeasurement");
function channelName(index2) {
  return `ch${(index2 + 1).toString().padStart(2, "0")}`;
}
__name(channelName, "channelName");

// src/ingest/acceptBatch.ts
async function acceptTmBatchV1(input) {
  const acceptedAt = /* @__PURE__ */ new Date();
  const rawPayloadSha256 = await sha256Hex(input.rawPayload);
  const rawR2Key = buildRawBatchObjectKey(input.batch);
  const batchMetadata = buildBatchMetadataInput(
    input.batch,
    rawR2Key,
    rawPayloadSha256,
    acceptedAt
  );
  const existingBatch = await loadIngestBatchByDeviceAndBatchId(
    input.database,
    input.batch.device_id,
    input.batch.batch_id
  );
  if (existingBatch !== null) {
    if (!isSameBatchMetadata(existingBatch, batchMetadata)) {
      return duplicateConflict();
    }
    const existingStatus = parseIngestBatchStatus(existingBatch.status);
    if (existingStatus === null) {
      return duplicateConflict();
    }
    if (existingStatus !== INGEST_BATCH_STATUS.accepted) {
      const rawArchiveResult2 = await storeOrConfirmRawArchive(
        input.rawBatchBucket,
        input.batch,
        input.rawPayload,
        batchMetadata
      );
      if (rawArchiveResult2 === "conflict") {
        return duplicateConflict();
      }
    }
    await finishAndAcceptBatch(
      input.database,
      input.batch,
      batchMetadata,
      acceptedAt,
      existingStatus !== INGEST_BATCH_STATUS.accepted
    );
    return { accepted: true };
  }
  const rawArchiveResult = await storeOrConfirmRawArchive(
    input.rawBatchBucket,
    input.batch,
    input.rawPayload,
    batchMetadata
  );
  if (rawArchiveResult === "conflict") {
    return duplicateConflict();
  }
  const metadataResult = await insertOrConfirmBatchMetadata(
    input.database,
    batchMetadata
  );
  if (!metadataResult.ready) {
    return duplicateConflict();
  }
  await finishAndAcceptBatch(
    input.database,
    input.batch,
    batchMetadata,
    acceptedAt,
    metadataResult.status !== INGEST_BATCH_STATUS.accepted
  );
  return { accepted: true };
}
__name(acceptTmBatchV1, "acceptTmBatchV1");
async function finishAndAcceptBatch(database, batch, batchMetadata, acceptedAt, markFailedOnError) {
  try {
    await finishBatchSideEffects(database, batch, acceptedAt);
    const markedAccepted = await updateIngestBatchStatus(database, {
      deviceId: batchMetadata.deviceId,
      batchId: batchMetadata.batchId,
      status: INGEST_BATCH_STATUS.accepted,
      onlyFrom: [...INGEST_BATCH_STATUSES]
    });
    if (!markedAccepted) {
      throw new Error("Unable to mark ingest batch as accepted");
    }
  } catch (error51) {
    if (markFailedOnError) {
      await markBatchFailedBestEffort(database, batchMetadata);
    }
    throw error51;
  }
}
__name(finishAndAcceptBatch, "finishAndAcceptBatch");
async function finishBatchSideEffects(database, batch, acceptedAt) {
  await insertMeasurementRows(database, {
    measurements: expandTmBatchV1ToMeasurements(batch),
    createdAt: acceptedAt
  });
  await updateDeviceIngestState(database, {
    deviceId: batch.device_id,
    seenAt: acceptedAt,
    seqLastAccepted: batch.seq_last
  });
}
__name(finishBatchSideEffects, "finishBatchSideEffects");
async function markBatchFailedBestEffort(database, batchMetadata) {
  try {
    await updateIngestBatchStatus(database, {
      deviceId: batchMetadata.deviceId,
      batchId: batchMetadata.batchId,
      status: INGEST_BATCH_STATUS.failed,
      onlyFrom: [
        INGEST_BATCH_STATUS.processing,
        INGEST_BATCH_STATUS.failed
      ]
    });
  } catch {
  }
}
__name(markBatchFailedBestEffort, "markBatchFailedBestEffort");
function buildBatchMetadataInput(batch, rawR2Key, rawPayloadSha256, receivedAt) {
  return {
    deviceId: batch.device_id,
    profile: batch.profile,
    batchId: batch.batch_id,
    seqFirst: batch.seq_first,
    seqLast: batch.seq_last,
    receivedAt,
    rawR2Key,
    rawPayloadSha256
  };
}
__name(buildBatchMetadataInput, "buildBatchMetadataInput");
async function insertOrConfirmBatchMetadata(database, batchMetadata) {
  const insertResult = await insertIngestBatch(database, {
    ...batchMetadata,
    status: INGEST_BATCH_STATUS.processing
  });
  if (insertResult.inserted) {
    return {
      ready: true,
      status: INGEST_BATCH_STATUS.processing
    };
  }
  const existingBatch = await loadIngestBatchByDeviceAndBatchId(
    database,
    batchMetadata.deviceId,
    batchMetadata.batchId
  );
  if (existingBatch !== null && isSameBatchMetadata(existingBatch, batchMetadata)) {
    const existingStatus = parseIngestBatchStatus(existingBatch.status);
    if (existingStatus !== null) {
      return { ready: true, status: existingStatus };
    }
  }
  return { ready: false, reason: "conflict" };
}
__name(insertOrConfirmBatchMetadata, "insertOrConfirmBatchMetadata");
async function storeOrConfirmRawArchive(bucket, batch, rawPayload, batchMetadata) {
  try {
    await storeRawBatchPayload(bucket, batch, rawPayload);
    return "ready";
  } catch (error51) {
    if (error51 instanceof RawBatchAlreadyArchivedError) {
      if (error51.objectKey !== batchMetadata.rawR2Key) {
        return "conflict";
      }
      return confirmExistingRawArchive(bucket, batchMetadata);
    }
    throw error51;
  }
}
__name(storeOrConfirmRawArchive, "storeOrConfirmRawArchive");
async function confirmExistingRawArchive(bucket, batchMetadata) {
  const archivedPayload = await loadRawBatchPayload(
    bucket,
    batchMetadata.rawR2Key
  );
  if (archivedPayload === null) {
    return "conflict";
  }
  const archivedPayloadSha256 = await sha256Hex(archivedPayload);
  if (archivedPayloadSha256 !== batchMetadata.rawPayloadSha256) {
    return "conflict";
  }
  return "ready";
}
__name(confirmExistingRawArchive, "confirmExistingRawArchive");
function isSameBatchMetadata(existingBatch, expectedBatch) {
  return existingBatch.deviceId === expectedBatch.deviceId && existingBatch.profile === expectedBatch.profile && existingBatch.batchId === expectedBatch.batchId && existingBatch.seqFirst === expectedBatch.seqFirst && existingBatch.seqLast === expectedBatch.seqLast && existingBatch.rawR2Key === expectedBatch.rawR2Key && existingBatch.rawPayloadSha256 === expectedBatch.rawPayloadSha256;
}
__name(isSameBatchMetadata, "isSameBatchMetadata");
function parseIngestBatchStatus(status) {
  for (const knownStatus of INGEST_BATCH_STATUSES) {
    if (status === knownStatus) {
      return knownStatus;
    }
  }
  return null;
}
__name(parseIngestBatchStatus, "parseIngestBatchStatus");
function duplicateConflict() {
  return { accepted: false, reason: "duplicate_batch_conflict" };
}
__name(duplicateConflict, "duplicateConflict");

// src/ingest/ack.ts
function buildAcceptedAck(batch, configRevision, cloudTime) {
  return {
    status: "accepted",
    device_id: batch.device_id,
    batch_id: batch.batch_id,
    accepted_seq_last: batch.seq_last,
    cloud_time: toUnixSeconds(cloudTime),
    config_revision: configRevision
  };
}
__name(buildAcceptedAck, "buildAcceptedAck");

// src/ingest/auth.ts
async function verifyDeviceToken(database, deviceId, suppliedToken) {
  const device = await loadActiveDeviceByDeviceId(database, deviceId);
  if (device === null) {
    return { ok: false, reason: "device_not_found" };
  }
  const suppliedTokenHash = await sha256Hex(suppliedToken);
  if (suppliedTokenHash !== device.tokenHash) {
    return { ok: false, reason: "invalid_token" };
  }
  return {
    ok: true,
    device: {
      deviceId: device.deviceId,
      configRevision: device.configRevision,
      lastSeqAccepted: device.lastSeqAccepted
    }
  };
}
__name(verifyDeviceToken, "verifyDeviceToken");

var TM_BATCH_SCHEMA_V1 = "tm.batch.v1";
var TM_PROFILE_V1_VW8_SHZK16_ENV_POWER = "tm.v1.vw8_shzk16_env_power";

  vibratingWire: {
    frequencyChannels: 8,
    temperatureChannels: 8
  },
  shzk: {
    temperatureChannels: 16
  },
  environmentFields: ["t_c", "rh_pct", "p_pa"],

// src/ingest/validate.ts
var supportedProfile = TM_V1_VW8_SHZK16_ENV_POWER_PROFILE;
var measurementValueSchema = external_exports.number().nullable();
var permissiveDiagnosticObjectSchema = external_exports.record(
  external_exports.string().max(TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxDiagnosticKeyLength),
  external_exports.unknown()
).superRefine((diagnostic, context) => {
  if (Object.keys(diagnostic).length > TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxDiagnosticKeys) {
    context.addIssue({
      code: "custom",
      message: `diagnostic object must have ${TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxDiagnosticKeys} keys or fewer`
    });
  }
  if (jsonByteLength(diagnostic) > TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxDiagnosticJsonBytes) {
    context.addIssue({
      code: "custom",
      message: `diagnostic object must be ${TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxDiagnosticJsonBytes} bytes or smaller`
    });
  }
});
var eventsSchema = external_exports.array(external_exports.unknown()).max(TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxEvents).superRefine((events, context) => {
  if (jsonByteLength(events) > TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxEventsJsonBytes) {
    context.addIssue({
      code: "custom",
      message: `events must be ${TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxEventsJsonBytes} bytes or smaller`
    });
  }
});
function requiredString(maxLength) {
  return external_exports.string().min(1).max(maxLength);
}
__name(requiredString, "requiredString");
function measurementArray(length) {
  return external_exports.array(measurementValueSchema).length(length);
}
__name(measurementArray, "measurementArray");
var tmBatchV1SampleSchema = external_exports.object({
  seq: external_exports.number().int(),
  t: external_exports.number().int().nullable(),
  vw_f: measurementArray(supportedProfile.vibratingWire.frequencyChannels),
  vw_t: measurementArray(supportedProfile.vibratingWire.temperatureChannels),
  shzk_t: measurementArray(supportedProfile.shzk.temperatureChannels),
  env: external_exports.object({
    t_c: measurementValueSchema,
    rh_pct: measurementValueSchema,
    p_pa: measurementValueSchema
  }).strict(),
  pwr: external_exports.object({
    vin_v: measurementValueSchema,
    iin_a: measurementValueSchema
  }).strict()
}).strict();
var tmBatchV1Schema = external_exports.object({
  schema: external_exports.literal(TM_BATCH_SCHEMA_V1),
  profile: external_exports.literal(TM_PROFILE_V1_VW8_SHZK16_ENV_POWER),
  device_id: requiredString(TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxIdentifierLength),
  batch_id: requiredString(TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxBatchIdLength),
  seq_first: external_exports.number().int(),
  seq_last: external_exports.number().int(),
  sample_period_s: external_exports.number().int(),
  created_at: external_exports.number().int(),
  boot_id: requiredString(TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxIdentifierLength),
  fw: requiredString(TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxVersionLength),
  hw: requiredString(TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxVersionLength),
  samples: external_exports.array(tmBatchV1SampleSchema).min(1).max(TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxSamples),
  state: permissiveDiagnosticObjectSchema,
  net: permissiveDiagnosticObjectSchema,
  queue: permissiveDiagnosticObjectSchema,
  events: eventsSchema
}).strict().superRefine((batch, context) => {
  if (batch.seq_first > batch.seq_last) {
    context.addIssue({
      code: "custom",
      path: ["seq_first"],
      message: "seq_first must be less than or equal to seq_last"
    });
  }
  if (batch.seq_first <= batch.seq_last && batch.seq_last - batch.seq_first > TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxSequenceGap) {
    context.addIssue({
      code: "custom",
      path: ["seq_last"],
      message: `seq_last must be within ${TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxSequenceGap} of seq_first`
    });
  }
  for (const [index2, sample] of batch.samples.entries()) {
    if (sample.seq < batch.seq_first || sample.seq > batch.seq_last) {
      context.addIssue({
        code: "custom",
        path: ["samples", index2, "seq"],
        message: "sample seq must be within seq_first and seq_last"
      });
    }
  }
});
var TmBatchValidationError = class extends Error {
  static {
    __name(this, "TmBatchValidationError");
  }
  issues;
  constructor(error51) {
    super(`Invalid tm.batch.v1 payload: ${formatZodIssues(error51)}`);
    this.name = "TmBatchValidationError";
    this.issues = error51.issues;
  }
};
function parseTmBatchV1(input) {
  const result = safeParseTmBatchV1(input);
  if (!result.success) {
    throw result.error;
  }
  return result.data;
}
__name(parseTmBatchV1, "parseTmBatchV1");
function safeParseTmBatchV1(input) {
  const result = tmBatchV1Schema.safeParse(input);
  if (result.success) {
    return { success: true, data: result.data };
  }
  return { success: false, error: new TmBatchValidationError(result.error) };
}
__name(safeParseTmBatchV1, "safeParseTmBatchV1");
function formatZodIssues(error51) {
  return error51.issues.map((issue2) => {
    const path = issue2.path.length > 0 ? issue2.path.join(".") : "<root>";
    return `${path}: ${issue2.message}`;
  }).join("; ");
}
__name(formatZodIssues, "formatZodIssues");
function jsonByteLength(value) {
  const json2 = JSON.stringify(value) ?? "null";
  return new TextEncoder().encode(json2).byteLength;
}
__name(jsonByteLength, "jsonByteLength");

// src/routes/ingest.ts
async function handleIngest(c) {
  const contentType = c.req.header("Content-Type") ?? "";
  if (!contentType.toLowerCase().includes("application/json")) {
    return c.json({ status: "rejected", reason: "unsupported_media_type" }, 415);
  }
  if (contentLengthExceedsLimit(c.req.raw, TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxRawBodyBytes)) {
    return c.json({ status: "rejected", reason: "payload_too_large" }, 413);
  }
  const deviceId = c.req.header("X-TM-Device");
  const suppliedToken = c.req.header("X-TM-Token");
  if (deviceId === void 0 || suppliedToken === void 0) {
    return c.json({ status: "rejected", reason: "unauthorized" }, 401);
  }
  const authResult = await verifyDeviceToken(c.env.DB, deviceId, suppliedToken);
  if (!authResult.ok) {
    return c.json({ status: "rejected", reason: "unauthorized" }, 401);
  }
  let rawPayload;
  try {
    rawPayload = await readTextBodyWithLimit(
      c.req.raw,
      TM_BATCH_V1_LIMITS.maxRawBodyBytes
    );
  } catch (error51) {
    if (error51 instanceof RequestBodyTooLargeError) {
      return c.json({ status: "rejected", reason: "payload_too_large" }, 413);
    }
    throw error51;
  }
  let batch;
  try {
    batch = parseTmBatchV1(JSON.parse(rawPayload));
  } catch (error51) {
    if (error51 instanceof SyntaxError || error51 instanceof TmBatchValidationError) {
      return c.json({ status: "rejected", reason: "invalid_payload" }, 400);
    }
    throw error51;
  }
  if (batch.device_id !== authResult.device.deviceId) {
    return c.json({ status: "rejected", reason: "device_mismatch" }, 403);
  }
  const acceptanceResult = await acceptTmBatchV1({
    database: c.env.DB,
    rawBatchBucket: c.env.RAW_BATCHES,
    batch,
    rawPayload
  });
  if (!acceptanceResult.accepted) {
    return c.json(
      { status: "rejected", reason: acceptanceResult.reason },
      409
    );
  }
  return c.json(
    buildAcceptedAck(
      batch,
      authResult.device.configRevision,
      /* @__PURE__ */ new Date()
    )
  );
}
__name(handleIngest, "handleIngest");

};

// src/routes/system.ts
var SERVICE_NAME = "TunnelMonitor";
var API_VERSION_V1 = "v1";
var RAW_ARCHIVE_HEALTHCHECK_KEY = "__healthcheck__/raw-archive";
function handleServiceInfo(c) {
  const releaseId = normalizeOptionalText(c.env.TM_RELEASE_ID);
  return c.json({
    service: SERVICE_NAME,
    version: package_default.version,
    ...releaseId === null ? {} : { release_id: releaseId },
    api_versions: [API_VERSION_V1],
    ingest_schemas: [TM_BATCH_SCHEMA_V1],
    links: {
      health: "/health",
      readiness: "/health/ready",
      database_health: "/health/db",
      raw_archive_health: "/health/storage",
      ingest: "/api/v1/ingest",
      admin_health: "/api/v1/admin/health"
    }
  });
}
__name(handleServiceInfo, "handleServiceInfo");
function handleHealth(c) {
  return c.json({ status: "ok" });
}
__name(handleHealth, "handleHealth");
async function handleDatabaseHealth(c) {
  const database = await checkDatabase(c.env.DB);
  if (database === "reachable") {
    return c.json({ status: "ok", database });
  }
  return c.json({ status: "error", database }, 503);
}
__name(handleDatabaseHealth, "handleDatabaseHealth");
async function handleStorageHealth(c) {
  const storage = await checkRawArchive(c.env.RAW_BATCHES);
  if (storage === "reachable") {
    return c.json({ status: "ok", storage });
  }
  return c.json({ status: "error", storage }, 503);
}
__name(handleStorageHealth, "handleStorageHealth");
async function handleReadiness(c) {
  const [database, rawArchive] = await Promise.all([
    checkDatabase(c.env.DB),
    checkRawArchive(c.env.RAW_BATCHES)
  ]);
  const ready = database === "reachable" && rawArchive === "reachable";
  return c.json(
    {
      status: ready ? "ready" : "not_ready",
      database,
      storage: rawArchive
    },
    ready ? 200 : 503
  );
}
__name(handleReadiness, "handleReadiness");
async function checkDatabase(database) {
  try {
    await database.prepare("SELECT 1").first();
    return "reachable";
  } catch {
    return "unreachable";
  }
}
__name(checkDatabase, "checkDatabase");
async function checkRawArchive(bucket) {
  try {
    await bucket.head(RAW_ARCHIVE_HEALTHCHECK_KEY);
    return "reachable";
  } catch {
    return "unreachable";
  }
}
__name(checkRawArchive, "checkRawArchive");
function normalizeOptionalText(value) {
  const normalized = value?.trim();
  if (normalized === void 0 || normalized.length === 0) {
    return null;
  }
  return normalized;
}
__name(normalizeOptionalText, "normalizeOptionalText");

// src/index.ts
var app = new Hono2();
app.get("/", handleServiceInfo);
app.get("/health", handleHealth);
app.get("/health/db", handleDatabaseHealth);
app.get("/health/storage", handleStorageHealth);
app.get("/health/ready", handleReadiness);
registerAdminUiRoutes(app);
app.post("/api/v1/ingest", handleIngest);
registerAdminRoutes(app);
var index_default = app;
export {
  index_default as default
};
//# sourceMappingURL=index.js.map
